```c
static int cmd_pid(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (strncmp(subcmd, "add ", 4) == 0) {
        pid_t pid;
        int i;
        if (kstrtoint(subcmd + 4, 10, &pid) != 0 || pid <= 0)
            return json_err(out, len, "pid add", "invalid pid");

        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        if (g_config.target_pid_count >= MAX_TARGET_PIDS) {
            spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
            return json_err(out, len, "pid add", "pid list full");
        }
        /* 检查重复 */
        for (i = 0; i < g_config.target_pid_count; i++) {
            if (g_config.target_pids[i] == pid) {
                spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
                return json_err(out, len, "pid add", "pid already exists");
            }
        }
        g_config.target_pids[g_config.target_pid_count++] = pid;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "pid add", "\"pid\":%d", pid);

    } else if (strncmp(subcmd, "remove ", 7) == 0) {
        pid_t pid;
        int i, found = 0;
        if (kstrtoint(subcmd + 7, 10, &pid) != 0)
            return json_err(out, len, "pid remove", "invalid pid");

        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        for (i = 0; i < g_config.target_pid_count; i++) {
            if (g_config.target_pids[i] == pid) {
                /* 将后续元素前移 */
                int j;
                for (j = i; j < g_config.target_pid_count - 1; j++)
                    g_config.target_pids[j] = g_config.target_pids[j + 1];
                g_config.target_pid_count--;
                found = 1;
                break;
            }
        }
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        if (!found)
            return json_err(out, len, "pid remove", "pid not found");
        return json_ok(out, len, "pid remove", "\"pid\":%d", pid);

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "clear") == 0) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.target_pid_count = 0;
        memset(g_config.target_pids, 0, sizeof(g_config.target_pids));
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "pid clear", "all pids cleared");

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "list") == 0) {
        int i, n;
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        n = snprintf(out, len,
            "{\"status\":\"ok\",\"command\":\"pid list\","
            "\"data\":{\"count\":%d,\"pids\":[",
            g_config.target_pid_count);
        for (i = 0; i < g_config.target_pid_count && n < len; i++) {
            if (i > 0) n += snprintf(out + n, len - n, ",");
            n += snprintf(out + n, len - n, "%d", g_config.target_pids[i]);
        }
        if (n < len) n += snprintf(out + n, len - n, "]}}");
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return 0;
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "pid", "unknown subcommand");
}

static int cmd_uid(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (strncmp(subcmd, "set ", 4) == 0) {
        unsigned int uid;
        if (kstrtouint(subcmd + 4, 10, &uid) != 0)
            return json_err(out, len, "uid set", "invalid uid");
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.target_uid = uid;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "uid set", "\"uid\":%u", uid);

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "clear") == 0) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.target_uid = 0xFFFFFFFF;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "uid clear", "uid filter cleared");
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "uid", "unknown subcommand");
}

static int cmd_app(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (strncmp(subcmd, "set ", 4) == 0) {
        const char *pkg = subcmd + 4;
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        strncpy(g_config.target_pkg, pkg, MAX_PKG_LEN - 1);
        g_config.target_pkg[MAX_PKG_LEN - 1] = '\0';
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "app set",
            "\"package\":\"%s\"", g_config.target_pkg);

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "clear") == 0) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.target_pkg[0] = '\0';
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "app clear", "app filter cleared");
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "app", "unknown subcommand");
}

static int cmd_comm(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (strncmp(subcmd, "set ", 4) == 0) {
        const char *comm = subcmd + 4;
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        strncpy(g_config.target_comm, comm, MAX_COMM_LEN - 1);
        g_config.target_comm[MAX_COMM_LEN - 1] = '\0';
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "comm set",
            "\"comm\":\"%s\"", g_config.target_comm);

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "clear") == 0) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.target_comm[0] = '\0';
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "comm clear", "comm filter cleared");
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "comm", "unknown subcommand");
}

/* --- 过滤配置命令 --- */

static int cmd_syscall(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (strncmp(subcmd, "add ", 4) == 0) {
        int nr;
        if (kstrtoint(subcmd + 4, 10, &nr) != 0 || nr < 0 || nr >= 320)
            return json_err(out, len, "syscall add", "invalid nr");
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        set_syscall_mask(nr, true);
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "syscall add",
            "\"nr\":%d,\"name\":\"%s\"", nr, get_syscall_name(nr));

    } else if (strncmp(subcmd, "remove ", 7) == 0) {
        int nr;
        if (kstrtoint(subcmd + 7, 10, &nr) != 0 || nr < 0 || nr >= 320)
            return json_err(out, len, "syscall remove", "invalid nr");
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        set_syscall_mask(nr, false);
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "syscall remove", "\"nr\":%d", nr);

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "clear") == 0) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.syscall_mask_lo = 0;
        g_config.syscall_mask_hi = 0;
        g_config.syscall_mask_x1 = 0;
        g_config.syscall_mask_x2 = 0;
        g_config.syscall_mask_x3 = 0;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "syscall clear", "all syscalls cleared");

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "list") == 0) {
        int i, n, first = 1;
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        n = snprintf(out, len,
            "{\"status\":\"ok\",\"command\":\"syscall list\","
            "\"data\":{\"syscalls\":[");
        for (i = 0; i < 320 && n < len - 64; i++) {
            if (is_syscall_masked(i)) {
                const char *name = get_syscall_name(i);
                if (name) {
                    if (!first) n += snprintf(out + n, len - n, ",");
                    n += snprintf(out + n, len - n,
                        "{\"nr\":%d,\"name\":\"%s\"}", i, name);
                    first = 0;
                }
            }
        }
        if (n < len) n += snprintf(out + n, len - n, "]}}");
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return 0;
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "syscall", "unknown subcommand");
}

static int cmd_cat(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (strncmp(subcmd, "set ", 4) == 0) {
        unsigned int mask;
        if (kstrtouint(subcmd + 4, 0, &mask) != 0)
            return json_err(out, len, "cat set", "invalid mask");
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.category_mask = (u8)(mask & 0x1F);
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "cat set", "\"mask\":\"0x%02x\"",
            g_config.category_mask);

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "reset") == 0) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.category_mask = SC_CAT_ALL;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "cat reset", "all categories enabled");
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "cat", "unknown subcommand");
}

static int cmd_range(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (strncmp(subcmd, "set ", 4) == 0) {
        int min_nr, max_nr;
        if (sscanf(subcmd + 4, "%d %d", &min_nr, &max_nr) != 2)
            return json_err(out, len, "range set", "usage: range set <min> <max>");
        if (min_nr < 0 || max_nr < min_nr || max_nr >= 320)
            return json_err(out, len, "range set", "invalid range");
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.syscall_range_min = min_nr;
        g_config.syscall_range_max = max_nr;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "range set",
            "\"min\":%d,\"max\":%d", min_nr, max_nr);
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "range", "unknown subcommand");
}

/* --- 日志配置命令 --- */

static int cmd_filelog(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (strcmp(subcmd, "enable") == 0) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.file_log_enabled = true;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        file_logger_init(g_config.file_log_path);
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "filelog enable", "file logging enabled");

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "disable") == 0) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.file_log_enabled = false;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        file_logger_cleanup();
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "filelog disable", "file logging disabled");

    } else if (strncmp(subcmd, "path ", 5) == 0) {
        const char *path = subcmd + 5;
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        strncpy(g_config.file_log_path, path, MAX_PATH_LEN - 1);
        g_config.file_log_path[MAX_PATH_LEN - 1] = '\0';
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "filelog path",
            "\"path\":\"%s\"", g_config.file_log_path);

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "truncate") == 0) {
        file_logger_truncate();
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "filelog truncate", "log file truncated");
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "filelog", "unknown subcommand");
}

static int cmd_option(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    bool val;

    /* 解析 on/off */
    const char *space = strchr(subcmd, ' ');
    if (!space)
        return json_err(out, len, "option", "usage: <option> on|off");

    int name_len = space - subcmd;
    const char *val_str = space + 1;

    if (strcmp(val_str, "on") == 0)       val = true;
    else if (strcmp(val_str, "off") == 0) val = false;
    else return json_err(out, len, "option", "value must be on or off");

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);

    if (strncmp(subcmd, "args", name_len) == 0 && name_len == 4)
        g_config.log_args = val;
    else if (strncmp(subcmd, "caller", name_len) == 0 && name_len == 6)
        g_config.log_caller = val;
    else if (strncmp(subcmd, "bt", name_len) == 0 && name_len == 2)
        g_config.log_backtrace = val;
    else if (strncmp(subcmd, "retval", name_len) == 0 && name_len == 6)
        g_config.log_retval = val;
    else if (strncmp(subcmd, "antidebug", name_len) == 0 && name_len == 9)
        g_config.antidebug_detect = val;
    else {
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_err(out, len, "option", "unknown option name");
    }

    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
    return json_ok_msg(out, len, subcmd, val ? "enabled" : "disabled");
}

/* --- 数据读取命令 --- */

static int cmd_log(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    if (strncmp(subcmd, "read", 4) == 0) {
        int count = 1;
        int n, i;
        struct svc_event ev;

        /* 解析可选的 count 参数 */
        if (subcmd[4] == ' ')
            kstrtoint(subcmd + 5, 10, &count);
        if (count <= 0) count = 1;
        if (count > 64) count = 64;

        n = snprintf(out, len,
            "{\"status\":\"ok\",\"command\":\"log read\","
            "\"data\":{\"events\":[");

        for (i = 0; i < count && n < len - 512; i++) {
            if (event_logger_pop(&ev) != 0) break;

            if (i > 0) n += snprintf(out + n, len - n, ",");
            n += snprintf(out + n, len - n,
                "{\"ts\":%llu,"
                "\"pid\":%d,\"tgid\":%d,\"uid\":%u,"
                "\"comm\":\"%s\","
                "\"nr\":%d,\"name\":\"%s\","
                "\"cat\":\"%s\","
                "\"ret\":%ld,"
                "\"pc\":\"0x%llx\",\"lr\":\"0x%llx\","
                "\"module\":\"%s\",\"offset\":\"0x%llx\","
                "\"detail\":\"%s\","
                "\"antidebug\":%s}",
                ev.timestamp_ns,
                ev.pid, ev.tgid, ev.uid,
                ev.comm,
                ev.syscall_nr, get_syscall_name(ev.syscall_nr),
                ev.category == SC_CAT_FILE ? "FILE" :
                ev.category == SC_CAT_PROC ? "PROC" :
                ev.category == SC_CAT_MEM  ? "MEM"  :
                ev.category == SC_CAT_NET  ? "NET"  :
                ev.category == SC_CAT_IPC  ? "IPC"  : "OTHER",
                ev.ret_val,
                ev.caller_pc, ev.caller_lr,
                ev.caller_module, ev.caller_offset,
                ev.detail,
                ev.is_antidebug ? "true" : "false");
        }

        if (n < len)
            n += snprintf(out + n, len - n,
                "],\"count\":%d,\"remaining\":%d}}",
                i, event_logger_count());
        return 0;

    } else if (strcmp(subcmd, "clear") == 0) {
        event_logger_clear();
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "log clear", "event buffer cleared");
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "log", "unknown subcommand");
}

static int cmd_maps(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    if (strcmp(subcmd, "clear") == 0) {
        maps_cache_clear();
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "maps clear", "maps cache cleared");

    } else if (strncmp(subcmd, "refresh", 7) == 0) {
        int i;
        unsigned long flags;
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        for (i = 0; i < g_config.target_pid_count; i++)
            maps_cache_refresh(g_config.target_pids[i]);
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok_msg(out, len, "maps refresh", "maps refreshed");
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "maps", "unknown subcommand");
}

/* --- 高级功能命令 --- */

static int cmd_hook(const char *subcmd, char *out, int len)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (strncmp(subcmd, "mode ", 5) == 0) {
        const char *mode = subcmd + 5;
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        if (strcmp(mode, "slim") == 0)
            g_config.hook_mode = HOOK_MODE_SLIM;
        else if (strcmp(mode, "all") == 0)
            g_config.hook_mode = HOOK_MODE_ALL;
        else if (strcmp(mode, "range") == 0)
            g_config.hook_mode = HOOK_MODE_RANGE;
        else {
            spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
            return json_err(out, len, "hook mode",
                "unknown mode (slim|all|range)");
        }
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return json_ok(out, len, "hook mode", "\"mode\":\"%s\"", mode);
    }

    return json_err(out, len, "hook", "unknown subcommand");
}

static int cmd_config_dump(char *out, int len)
{
    /* 将当前配置以可恢复的格式输出 */
    unsigned long flags;
    int n;
    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
    n = snprintf(out, len,
        "{\"status\":\"ok\",\"command\":\"config dump\","
        "\"data\":{"
        "\"active\":%s,"
        "\"target_uid\":%u,"
        "\"target_pkg\":\"%s\","
        "\"target_comm\":\"%s\","
        "\"hook_mode\":%d,"
        "\"category_mask\":%u,"
        "\"range_min\":%d,\"range_max\":%d,"
        "\"log_args\":%s,"
        "\"log_caller\":%s,"
        "\"log_backtrace\":%s,"
        "\"log_retval\":%s,"
        "\"antidebug\":%s,"
        "\"json_output\":%s,"
        "\"file_log\":%s,"
        "\"file_path\":\"%s\""
        "}}",
        g_config.active ? "true" : "false",
        g_config.target_uid,
        g_config.target_pkg,
        g_config.target_comm,
        g_config.hook_mode,
        g_config.category_mask,
        g_config.syscall_range_min, g_config.syscall_range_max,
        g_config.log_args ? "true" : "false",
        g_config.log_caller ? "true" : "false",
        g_config.log_backtrace ? "true" : "false",
        g_config.log_retval ? "true" : "false",
        g_config.antidebug_detect ? "true" : "false",
        g_config.json_output ? "true" : "false",
        g_config.file_log_enabled ? "true" : "false",
        g_config.file_log_path);
    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
    return 0;
}

/* ============================================================
 * KPM 生命周期函数
 * ============================================================ */

long kpm_init(const char *args, const char *event, void *reserved)
{
    int ret;

    pr_info("[%s] initializing v%s\n", MODULE_NAME, SVC_TRACER_VERSION);

    /* 设置默认配置（无默认包名） */
    config_set_defaults();

    /* 初始化符号解析器（必须最先） */
    ret = symbol_resolver_init();
    if (ret) {
        pr_err("[%s] symbol_resolver_init failed: %d\n", MODULE_NAME, ret);
        return ret;
    }

    /* 初始化事件缓冲区 */
    ret = event_logger_init();
    if (ret) {
        pr_err("[%s] event_logger_init failed: %d\n", MODULE_NAME, ret);
        goto fail_event;
    }

    /* 初始化 maps 缓存 */
    ret = maps_cache_init();
    if (ret) {
        pr_err("[%s] maps_cache_init failed: %d\n", MODULE_NAME, ret);
        goto fail_maps;
    }

    /* 初始化包名解析器 */
    ret = pkg_resolver_init();
    if (ret) {
        pr_err("[%s] pkg_resolver_init failed: %d\n", MODULE_NAME, ret);
        goto fail_pkg;
    }

    /* 初始化 hook 引擎（注册但不启动） */
    ret = hook_engine_init();
    if (ret) {
        pr_err("[%s] hook_engine_init failed: %d\n", MODULE_NAME, ret);
        goto fail_hook;
    }

    /* 如果 args 中包含初始化参数，解析之 */
    if (args && args[0]) {
        /* 支持 "pkg=com.example.app" 格式的初始参数 */
        if (strncmp(args, "pkg=", 4) == 0) {
            unsigned long flags;
            spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
            strncpy(g_config.target_pkg, args + 4, MAX_PKG_LEN - 1);
            g_config.target_pkg[MAX_PKG_LEN - 1] = '\0';
            spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
            pr_info("[%s] initial target pkg: %s\n",
                MODULE_NAME, g_config.target_pkg);
        }
    }

    pr_info("[%s] initialized successfully, use ctl0 to configure\n",
        MODULE_NAME);
    return 0;

fail_hook:
    pkg_resolver_cleanup();
fail_pkg:
    maps_cache_cleanup();
fail_maps:
    event_logger_cleanup();
fail_event:
    symbol_resolver_cleanup();
    return ret;
}

long kpm_control0(const char *args, char *out_msg, int out_len)
{
    if (!args || !out_msg || out_len <= 0) {
        return -1;
    }

    /* 跳过前导空格 */
    while (*args == ' ') args++;

    /* ---- 状态管理命令 ---- */
    if (strcmp(args, "status") == 0)
        return cmd_status(out_msg, out_len);
    if (strcmp(args, "start") == 0)
        return cmd_start(out_msg, out_len);
    if (strcmp(args, "stop") == 0)
        return cmd_stop(out_msg, out_len);
    if (strcmp(args, "version") == 0)
        return cmd_version(out_msg, out_len);
    if (strcmp(args, "stats") == 0)
        return cmd_stats(out_msg, out_len);
    if (strcmp(args, "reset") == 0)
        return cmd_reset(out_msg, out_len);

    /* ---- 目标配置命令 ---- */
    if (strncmp(args, "pid ", 4) == 0)
        return cmd_pid(args + 4, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "uid ", 4) == 0)
        return cmd_uid(args + 4, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "app ", 4) == 0)
        return cmd_app(args + 4, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "comm ", 5) == 0)
        return cmd_comm(args + 5, out_msg, out_len);

    /* ---- 过滤配置命令 ---- */
    if (strncmp(args, "syscall ", 8) == 0)
        return cmd_syscall(args + 8, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "cat ", 4) == 0)
        return cmd_cat(args + 4, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "range ", 6) == 0)
        return cmd_range(args + 6, out_msg, out_len);

    /* ---- 日志配置命令 ---- */
    if (strncmp(args, "filelog ", 7) == 0)
        return cmd_filelog(args + 7, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "args ", 5) == 0)
        return cmd_option(args, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "caller ", 7) == 0)
        return cmd_option(args, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "bt ", 3) == 0)
        return cmd_option(args, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "retval ", 7) == 0)
        return cmd_option(args, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "antidebug ", 10) == 0)
        return cmd_option(args, out_msg, out_len);

    /* ---- 数据读取命令 ---- */
    if (strncmp(args, "log ", 4) == 0)
        return cmd_log(args + 4, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strncmp(args, "maps ", 5) == 0)
        return cmd_maps(args + 5, out_msg, out_len);

    /* ---- 高级功能命令 ---- */
    if (strncmp(args, "hook ", 5) == 0)
        return cmd_hook(args + 5, out_msg, out_len);
    if (strcmp(args, "config dump") == 0)
        return cmd_config_dump(out_msg, out_len);

    /* 未知命令 */
    return json_err(out_msg, out_len, args, "unknown command");
}

long kpm_exit(void *reserved)
{
    pr_info("[%s] unloading\n", MODULE_NAME);

    /* 停止监控 */
    g_config.active = false;
    hook_engine_stop();

    /* 按初始化相反顺序清理 */
    hook_engine_cleanup();
    file_logger_cleanup();
    pkg_resolver_cleanup();
    maps_cache_cleanup();
    event_logger_cleanup();
    symbol_resolver_cleanup();

    pr_info("[%s] unloaded\n", MODULE_NAME);
    return 0;
}

KPM_INIT(kpm_init);
KPM_CTL0(kpm_control0);
KPM_EXIT(kpm_exit);
```

---

## 4.3 hook_engine.c/.h 修改

### 4.3.1 修改原因和目的

原版 `hook_engine.c` 仅注册了约 14 个常用 syscall 的 hook，无法覆盖内存管理、网络通信、IPC 等重要类别的系统调用。改进版将 hook 扩展到 30+ 个 syscall，并使用统一的 pre/post 回调机制。

| 问题 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| Hook 数量不足 | 仅 14 个，缺少内存/网络/IPC 类 |
| 无分类管理 | 所有 hook 混在一起，无法按类别启停 |
| 无统一回调框架 | 每个 syscall 独立处理，代码重复 |

### 4.3.2 修改前的问题代码（简要引用）

```c
// 原版仅定义 14 个 hook
static struct syscall_hook_desc g_hooks[] = {
    { __NR_openat,      "openat",      4 },
    { __NR_read,        "read",        3 },
    { __NR_write,       "write",       3 },
    { __NR_close,       "close",       1 },
    { __NR_ioctl,       "ioctl",       3 },
    { __NR_faccessat,   "faccessat",   3 },
    { __NR_clone,       "clone",       5 },
    { __NR_execve,      "execve",      3 },
    { __NR_kill,        "kill",        2 },
    { __NR_ptrace,      "ptrace",      4 },
    { __NR_socket,      "socket",      3 },
    { __NR_connect,     "connect",     3 },
    { __NR_prctl,       "prctl",       5 },
    { __NR_clock_gettime, "clock_gettime", 2 },
};
```

### 4.3.3 修改方案说明

1. **扩展 g_hooks 到 35+ 个 syscall**，覆盖五大类别。
2. **每个 hook 条目增加 category 字段**，支持按类别过滤。
3. **统一 pre-hook 回调**：`generic_pre_handler()` 自动收集事件信息。
4. **统一 post-hook 回调**：`generic_post_handler()` 收集返回值并推送事件。
5. **支持 slim/all/range 三种 hook 模式**。

以下是 ARM64 上各 syscall 的 `__NR` 号码对照表（基于 Linux 5.10+ aarch64）：

| 类别 | Syscall | __NR | 参数数 |
|------|---------|------|--------|
| FILE | openat | 56 | 4 |
| FILE | close | 57 | 1 |
| FILE | read | 63 | 3 |
| FILE | write | 64 | 3 |
| FILE | readv | 65 | 3 |
| FILE | writev | 66 | 3 |
| FILE | ioctl | 29 | 3 |
| FILE | faccessat | 48 | 3 |
| FILE | fstat | 80 | 2 |
| FILE | lseek | 62 | 3 |
| FILE | dup | 23 | 1 |
| FILE | dup3 | 24 | 3 |
| FILE | pipe2 | 59 | 2 |
| PROC | clone | 220 | 5 |
| PROC | execve | 221 | 3 |
| PROC | kill | 129 | 2 |
| PROC | ptrace | 117 | 4 |
| PROC | prctl | 167 | 5 |
| PROC | wait4 | 260 | 4 |
| PROC | exit_group | 94 | 1 |
| PROC | getpid | 172 | 0 |
| PROC | getuid | 174 | 0 |
| MEM | mmap | 222 | 6 |
| MEM | munmap | 215 | 2 |
| MEM | mprotect | 226 | 3 |
| MEM | madvise | 233 | 3 |
| MEM | mremap | 216 | 5 |
| NET | socket | 198 | 3 |
| NET | connect | 203 | 3 |
| NET | sendto | 206 | 6 |
| NET | recvfrom | 207 | 6 |
| NET | bind | 200 | 3 |
| NET | listen | 201 | 2 |
| NET | accept4 | 242 | 4 |
| NET | setsockopt | 208 | 5 |
| NET | getsockname | 204 | 3 |
| IPC | epoll_create1 | 20 | 1 |
| IPC | epoll_ctl | 21 | 4 |
| IPC | eventfd2 | 19 | 2 |
| PROC | clock_gettime | 113 | 2 |

### 4.3.4 修改后的完整代码

**hook_engine.h**

```c
/* hook_engine.h — Syscall Hook 引擎头文件 */

#ifndef _HOOK_ENGINE_H_
#define _HOOK_ENGINE_H_

#include "svc_tracer.h"

/* Hook 引擎初始化（注册所有 hook 点，但不激活） */
int hook_engine_init(void);

/* 清理所有 hook */
void hook_engine_cleanup(void);

/* 启动/停止所有 hook */
int hook_engine_start(void);
void hook_engine_stop(void);

/* 查询已注册 hook 数量 */
int hook_engine_get_count(void);

/* 按 NR 查询 hook 描述 */
const struct syscall_hook_desc *hook_engine_get_desc(int nr);

/* 检查指定 NR 是否为 slim 模式核心 syscall */
bool hook_engine_is_slim(int nr);

#endif /* _HOOK_ENGINE_H_ */
```

**hook_engine.c**

```c
/* hook_engine.c — Syscall Hook 引擎实现
 *
 * 基于 KernelPatch 的 syscall hook 框架，注册并管理所有
 * 需要监控的 ARM64 系统调用。
 *
 * 核心机制：
 * - 使用 KPM 的 inline hook 或 SVC 拦截机制
 * - 统一的 pre/post handler 收集事件信息
 * - 支持 slim/all/range 三种 hook 模式
 */

#include <linux/kernel.h>
#include <linux/string.h>
#include <asm/unistd.h>
#include <kpm_hook.h>
#include <kpm_utils.h>
#include "svc_tracer.h"
#include "hook_engine.h"

/* ============================================================
 * Slim 模式核心 syscall 列表
 * 这些是最常需要监控的高价值 syscall
 * ============================================================ */
static const int slim_syscalls[] = {
    __NR_openat, __NR_close, __NR_read, __NR_write,
    __NR_ioctl, __NR_faccessat,
    __NR_clone, __NR_execve, __NR_kill, __NR_ptrace, __NR_prctl,
    __NR_mmap, __NR_mprotect,
    __NR_socket, __NR_connect,
    __NR_clock_gettime,
};
#define SLIM_COUNT (sizeof(slim_syscalls) / sizeof(slim_syscalls[0]))

/* ============================================================
 * 统一 Pre-Hook 处理函数
 *
 * 在 syscall 执行前调用，收集：
 * - 时间戳、PID/TGID/UID、comm
 * - syscall 编号和原始参数
 * - 调用者 PC/LR
 * ============================================================ */
static void generic_pre_handler(struct pt_regs *regs, int nr,
                                 struct svc_event *ev)
{
    struct task_struct *task = current;

    ev->timestamp_ns = ktime_get_ns();
    ev->pid = task->pid;
    ev->tgid = task->tgid;
    ev->uid = __kuid_val(task_uid(task));
    memcpy(ev->comm, task->comm, MAX_COMM_LEN);
    ev->comm[MAX_COMM_LEN - 1] = '\0';

    ev->syscall_nr = nr;
    ev->args[0] = regs->regs[0];  /* x0 */
    ev->args[1] = regs->regs[1];  /* x1 */
    ev->args[2] = regs->regs[2];  /* x2 */
    ev->args[3] = regs->regs[3];  /* x3 */
    ev->args[4] = regs->regs[4];  /* x4 */
    ev->args[5] = regs->regs[5];  /* x5 */

    ev->caller_pc = regs->pc;              /* ELR_EL1 */
    ev->caller_lr = regs->regs[30];        /* x30 = LR */

    ev->ret_val = 0;
    ev->backtrace_depth = 0;
    ev->is_antidebug = false;
    ev->detail[0] = '\0';
    ev->caller_module[0] = '\0';
    ev->caller_offset = 0;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 统一 Post-Hook 处理函数
 *
 * 在 syscall 执行后调用：
 * - 收集返回值
 * - 解析参数
 * - 检测反调试行为
 * - 解析调用者模块信息
 * - 栈回溯（如果启用）
 * - 推送事件到环形缓冲区
 * ============================================================ */
static void generic_post_handler(struct pt_regs *regs, struct svc_event *ev)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    bool should;

    /* 检查是否应该监控此进程 */
    should = should_monitor(ev->pid, ev->tgid, ev->uid, ev->comm);
    if (!should) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.stats.filtered_events++;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return;
    }

    /* 获取 syscall 类别 */
    ev->category = get_syscall_category(ev->syscall_nr);

    /* 检查类别过滤 */
    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
    if (!(g_config.category_mask & ev->category)) {
        g_config.stats.filtered_events++;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return;
    }

    /* 检查 syscall NR 掩码 */
    if (!is_syscall_masked(ev->syscall_nr)) {
        g_config.stats.filtered_events++;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
        return;
    }
    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);

    /* 收集返回值 */
    if (g_config.log_retval)
        ev->ret_val = regs->regs[0];

    /* 解析参数为可读字符串 */
    if (g_config.log_args)
        parse_args(ev->syscall_nr, ev->args, ev->detail, MAX_DETAIL_LEN);

    /* 反调试检测 */
    if (g_config.antidebug_detect)
        ev->is_antidebug = is_antidebug_behavior(
            ev->syscall_nr, ev->args, ev->detail);

    /* 解析调用者模块信息 */
    if (g_config.log_caller)
        resolve_caller(ev->caller_pc, ev->caller_lr, ev->tgid,
                       ev->caller_module, &ev->caller_offset);

    /* 栈回溯 */
    if (g_config.log_backtrace) {
        void *fp = (void *)regs->regs[29];  /* FP = x29 */
        ev->backtrace_depth = resolve_backtrace(
            fp, ev->tgid,
            ev->backtrace, ev->backtrace_symbols,
            MAX_STACK_DEPTH);
    }

    /* 更新统计 */
    stats_update(ev->category);

    /* 推送事件到环形缓冲区 */
    if (event_logger_push(ev) != 0) {
        spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);
        g_config.stats.dropped_events++;
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
    }

    /* 写入文件日志（如果启用） */
    if (g_config.file_log_enabled) {
        if (g_config.json_output)
            file_logger_write_event_json(ev);
        else
            file_logger_write_event(ev);
    }
}

/* ============================================================
 * 完整的 Syscall Hook 描述表（35 个）
 * ============================================================ */

/* 前向声明所有 hook handler */
static void svc_hook_handler(struct pt_regs *regs, int nr);

/*
 * g_hooks: 所有可 hook 的 syscall 描述表
 * 每个条目包含 NR、名称、参数数、类别
 */
static struct syscall_hook_desc g_hooks[] = {
    /* ---- FILE 类 (13个) ---- */
    { .nr = 56,  .name = "openat",      .arg_count = 4, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 57,  .name = "close",       .arg_count = 1, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 63,  .name = "read",        .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 64,  .name = "write",       .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 65,  .name = "readv",       .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 66,  .name = "writev",      .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 29,  .name = "ioctl",       .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 48,  .name = "faccessat",   .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 80,  .name = "fstat",       .arg_count = 2, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 62,  .name = "lseek",       .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 23,  .name = "dup",         .arg_count = 1, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 24,  .name = "dup3",        .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },
    { .nr = 59,  .name = "pipe2",       .arg_count = 2, .category = SC_CAT_FILE },

    /* ---- PROC 类 (10个) ---- */
    { .nr = 220, .name = "clone",       .arg_count = 5, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },
    { .nr = 221, .name = "execve",      .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },
    { .nr = 129, .name = "kill",        .arg_count = 2, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },
    { .nr = 117, .name = "ptrace",      .arg_count = 4, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },
    { .nr = 167, .name = "prctl",       .arg_count = 5, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },
    { .nr = 260, .name = "wait4",       .arg_count = 4, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },
    { .nr = 94,  .name = "exit_group",  .arg_count = 1, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },
    { .nr = 172, .name = "getpid",      .arg_count = 0, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },
    { .nr = 174, .name = "getuid",      .arg_count = 0, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },
    { .nr = 113, .name = "clock_gettime", .arg_count = 2, .category = SC_CAT_PROC },

    /* ---- MEM 类 (5个) ---- */
    { .nr = 222, .name = "mmap",        .arg_count = 6, .category = SC_CAT_MEM },
    { .nr = 215, .name = "munmap",      .arg_count = 2, .category = SC_CAT_MEM },
    { .nr = 226, .name = "mprotect",    .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_MEM },
    { .nr = 233, .name = "madvise",     .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_MEM },
    { .nr = 216, .name = "mremap",      .arg_count = 5, .category = SC_CAT_MEM },

    /* ---- NET 类 (9个) ---- */
    { .nr = 198, .name = "socket",      .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_NET },
    { .nr = 203, .name = "connect",     .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_NET },
    { .nr = 206, .name = "sendto",      .arg_count = 6, .category = SC_CAT_NET },
    { .nr = 207, .name = "recvfrom",    .arg_count = 6, .category = SC_CAT_NET },
    { .nr = 200, .name = "bind",        .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_NET },
    { .nr = 201, .name = "listen",      .arg_count = 2, .category = SC_CAT_NET },
    { .nr = 242, .name = "accept4",     .arg_count = 4, .category = SC_CAT_NET },
    { .nr = 208, .name = "setsockopt",  .arg_count = 5, .category = SC_CAT_NET },
    { .nr = 204, .name = "getsockname", .arg_count = 3, .category = SC_CAT_NET },

    /* ---- IPC 类 (3个) ---- */
    { .nr = 20,  .name = "epoll_create1", .arg_count = 1, .category = SC_CAT_IPC },
    { .nr = 21,  .name = "epoll_ctl",     .arg_count = 4, .category = SC_CAT_IPC },
    { .nr = 19,  .name = "eventfd2",      .arg_count = 2, .category = SC_CAT_IPC },
};

#define HOOK_COUNT (sizeof(g_hooks) / sizeof(g_hooks[0]))

/* Hook 安装状态数组 */
static bool g_hook_installed[HOOK_COUNT];
static bool g_hooks_active = false;

/* ============================================================
 * Hook 回调入口（KPM SVC 拦截）
 *
 * KPM 框架在 SVC 处理路径上调用此函数。
 * 使用 per-task 的 svc_event 存储（避免锁竞争）。
 * ============================================================ */

/* Per-CPU 事件暂存区（简化版，使用数组索引） */
#define MAX_CPUS 8
static struct svc_event g_per_cpu_events[MAX_CPUS];

static void svc_hook_handler(struct pt_regs *regs, int nr)
{
    int cpu;
    struct svc_event *ev;

    if (!g_hooks_active || !g_config.active)
        return;

    cpu = smp_processor_id() % MAX_CPUS;
    ev = &g_per_cpu_events[cpu];

    memset(ev, 0, sizeof(*ev));
    generic_pre_handler(regs, nr, ev);
    /* 注意：post_handler 将在 syscall 返回后由框架调用 */
}

static void svc_hook_post_handler(struct pt_regs *regs, int nr)
{
    int cpu;
    struct svc_event *ev;

    if (!g_hooks_active || !g_config.active)
        return;

    cpu = smp_processor_id() % MAX_CPUS;
    ev = &g_per_cpu_events[cpu];

    if (ev->syscall_nr == nr)
        generic_post_handler(regs, ev);
}

/* ============================================================
 * 查找 hook 描述
 * ============================================================ */
static int find_hook_index(int nr)
{
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < HOOK_COUNT; i++) {
        if (g_hooks[i].nr == nr)
            return i;
    }
    return -1;
}

bool hook_engine_is_slim(int nr)
{
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < SLIM_COUNT; i++) {
        if (slim_syscalls[i] == nr)
            return true;
    }
    return false;
}

const struct syscall_hook_desc *hook_engine_get_desc(int nr)
{
    int idx = find_hook_index(nr);
    if (idx < 0) return NULL;
    return &g_hooks[idx];
}

int hook_engine_get_count(void)
{
    return HOOK_COUNT;
}

/* ============================================================
 * Hook 引擎生命周期
 * ============================================================ */

int hook_engine_init(void)
{
    int i, ret;

    memset(g_hook_installed, 0, sizeof(g_hook_installed));
    memset(g_per_cpu_events, 0, sizeof(g_per_cpu_events));
    g_hooks_active = false;

    pr_info("[hook_engine] registering %d syscall hooks\n", (int)HOOK_COUNT);

    for (i = 0; i < HOOK_COUNT; i++) {
        /* 注册 hook 点但不激活 */
        ret = kpm_hook_syscall(g_hooks[i].nr,
                               svc_hook_handler,
                               svc_hook_post_handler);
        if (ret == 0) {
            g_hook_installed[i] = true;
        } else {
            pr_warn("[hook_engine] failed to register hook for %s (NR %d): %d\n",
                g_hooks[i].name, g_hooks[i].nr, ret);
            g_hook_installed[i] = false;
        }
    }

    return 0;
}

int hook_engine_start(void)
{
    int i, count = 0;
    int mode = g_config.hook_mode;

    for (i = 0; i < HOOK_COUNT; i++) {
        if (!g_hook_installed[i]) continue;

        bool should_activate = false;

        switch (mode) {
        case HOOK_MODE_SLIM:
            should_activate = hook_engine_is_slim(g_hooks[i].nr);
            break;
        case HOOK_MODE_ALL:
            should_activate = true;
            break;
        case HOOK_MODE_RANGE:
            should_activate = (g_hooks[i].nr >= g_config.syscall_range_min &&
                              g_hooks[i].nr <= g_config.syscall_range_max);
            break;
        }

        if (should_activate) {
            kpm_hook_enable(g_hooks[i].nr);
            count++;
        }
    }

    g_hooks_active = true;
    pr_info("[hook_engine] started, %d hooks active (mode=%d)\n", count, mode);
    return count;
}

void hook_engine_stop(void)
{
    int i;

    g_hooks_active = false;

    for (i = 0; i < HOOK_COUNT; i++) {
        if (g_hook_installed[i])
            kpm_hook_disable(g_hooks[i].nr);
    }

    pr_info("[hook_engine] stopped\n");
}

void hook_engine_cleanup(void)
{
    int i;

    hook_engine_stop();

    for (i = 0; i < HOOK_COUNT; i++) {
        if (g_hook_installed[i]) {
            kpm_hook_unhook(g_hooks[i].nr);
            g_hook_installed[i] = false;
        }
    }

    pr_info("[hook_engine] cleaned up\n");
}
```

---

## 4.4 syscall_monitor.c/.h 修改

### 4.4.1 修改原因和目的

原版 `syscall_monitor.c` 的过滤逻辑过于简单，反调试检测覆盖面不够，参数解析也仅支持少数 syscall。改进版需要：

| 问题 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| 过滤逻辑简单 | 仅支持单条件过滤，无 AND/OR 组合 |
| 反调试检测不全 | 缺少 /proc/self/fd 遍历、inotify、personality 等检测 |
| 参数解析不完整 | 新增的 30+ syscall 缺少对应的参数解析 |
| 无统计更新 | 没有集成统计计数器 |

### 4.4.2 修改前的问题代码（简要引用）

```c
// 原版 should_monitor 仅单条件
bool should_monitor(pid_t pid, pid_t tgid)
{
    if (g_config.target_pid != 0 && g_config.target_pid != pid)
        return false;
    if (g_config.target_tgid != 0 && g_config.target_tgid != tgid)
        return false;
    return true;
}

// 原版反调试检测 — 仅检查 ptrace 和部分 prctl
bool is_antidebug_behavior(int nr, u64 *args)
{
    if (nr == __NR_ptrace && args[0] == 0) return true;  // PTRACE_TRACEME
    if (nr == __NR_prctl && args[0] == 4)  return true;  // PR_SET_DUMPABLE(0)
    return false;
}
```

### 4.4.3 修改方案说明

1. **should_monitor() 多条件组合**：支持 PID 列表、TGID、UID、包名、comm 的 AND 组合过滤。至少一个目标条件被设置时，所有设置的条件必须同时满足。
2. **get_syscall_category() 扩展**：覆盖所有 35 个 hook 的 syscall。
3. **is_antidebug_behavior() 增强**：
   - `/proc/self/fd` 遍历检测
   - `inotify_add_watch` 对 `/proc/self` 的检测
   - `prctl PR_SET_PTRACER` 检测
   - `personality(ADDR_NO_RANDOMIZE)` 检测
   - `clock_gettime` 高频调用模式检测（timer-based 反调试）
4. **parse_args() 全覆盖**：为所有 35 个 syscall 编写参数解析逻辑。
5. **stats_update()**：按类别更新统计计数器。

### 4.4.4 修改后的完整代码

**syscall_monitor.h**

```c
/* syscall_monitor.h — Syscall 监控与过滤头文件 */

#ifndef _SYSCALL_MONITOR_H_
#define _SYSCALL_MONITOR_H_

#include "svc_tracer.h"

/* 判断是否应该监控指定进程 */
bool should_monitor(pid_t pid, pid_t tgid, uid_t uid, const char *comm);

/* 获取 syscall 类别 */
u8 get_syscall_category(int nr);

/* 获取 syscall 名称 */
const char *get_syscall_name(int nr);

/* 判断是否为反调试行为 */
bool is_antidebug_behavior(int nr, u64 *args, const char *detail);

/* 解析 syscall 参数为可读字符串 */
void parse_args(int nr, u64 *args, char *detail, int detail_len);

/* 更新统计计数器 */
void stats_update(u8 category);

#endif /* _SYSCALL_MONITOR_H_ */
```

**syscall_monitor.c**

```c
/* syscall_monitor.c — Syscall 监控与过滤实现
 *
 * 负责：
 * 1. 进程过滤（多条件 AND 组合）
 * 2. Syscall 分类
 * 3. 参数解析为可读格式
 * 4. 反调试行为检测
 * 5. 统计计数器维护
 */

#include <linux/kernel.h>
#include <linux/string.h>
#include <linux/sched.h>
#include <asm/unistd.h>
#include <kpm_utils.h>
#include "svc_tracer.h"
#include "syscall_monitor.h"

/* ============================================================
 * clock_gettime 高频检测相关
 * ============================================================ */
#define CLOCK_ANTIDEBUG_THRESHOLD   20   /* 100ms 内超过此次数视为可疑 */
#define CLOCK_ANTIDEBUG_WINDOW_NS   (100 * 1000 * 1000)  /* 100ms */

/* 简单的 per-tgid 时钟调用频率统计 */
struct clock_freq_entry {
    pid_t tgid;
    u64 first_call_ns;
    int call_count;
};

#define MAX_CLOCK_ENTRIES 16
static struct clock_freq_entry clock_freq[MAX_CLOCK_ENTRIES];
static spinlock_t clock_freq_lock;
static bool clock_freq_initialized = false;

static void clock_freq_init(void)
{
    if (!clock_freq_initialized) {
        spin_lock_init(&clock_freq_lock);
        memset(clock_freq, 0, sizeof(clock_freq));
        clock_freq_initialized = true;
    }
}

/* 检查 clock_gettime 是否为高频调用（反调试模式） */
static bool check_clock_antidebug(pid_t tgid)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    int i, free_slot = -1;
    u64 now = ktime_get_ns();
    bool suspicious = false;

    clock_freq_init();
    spin_lock_irqsave(&clock_freq_lock, flags);

    for (i = 0; i < MAX_CLOCK_ENTRIES; i++) {
        if (clock_freq[i].tgid == tgid) {
            /* 检查时间窗口 */
            if (now - clock_freq[i].first_call_ns > CLOCK_ANTIDEBUG_WINDOW_NS) {
                /* 重置窗口 */
                clock_freq[i].first_call_ns = now;
                clock_freq[i].call_count = 1;
            } else {
                clock_freq[i].call_count++;
                if (clock_freq[i].call_count >= CLOCK_ANTIDEBUG_THRESHOLD)
                    suspicious = true;
            }
            goto out;
        }
        if (clock_freq[i].tgid == 0 && free_slot < 0)
            free_slot = i;
    }

    /* 新条目 */
    if (free_slot >= 0) {
        clock_freq[free_slot].tgid = tgid;
        clock_freq[free_slot].first_call_ns = now;
        clock_freq[free_slot].call_count = 1;
    }

out:
    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&clock_freq_lock, flags);
    return suspicious;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 进程过滤: should_monitor()
 *
 * 多条件 AND 组合逻辑：
 * - 如果没有设置任何目标条件，返回 false（避免监控所有进程）
 * - 如果设置了某个条件，该条件必须匹配
 * - 所有已设置的条件必须同时满足
 * ============================================================ */
bool should_monitor(pid_t pid, pid_t tgid, uid_t uid, const char *comm)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    bool has_filter = false;
    bool pid_match = true;
    bool tgid_match = true;
    bool uid_match = true;
    bool pkg_match = true;
    bool comm_match = true;
    int i;

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);

    /* PID 列表过滤 */
    if (g_config.target_pid_count > 0) {
        has_filter = true;
        pid_match = false;
        for (i = 0; i < g_config.target_pid_count; i++) {
            if (g_config.target_pids[i] == pid ||
                g_config.target_pids[i] == tgid) {
                pid_match = true;
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    /* TGID 过滤 */
    if (g_config.target_tgid != 0) {
        has_filter = true;
        tgid_match = (g_config.target_tgid == tgid);
    }

    /* UID 过滤 */
    if (g_config.target_uid != 0xFFFFFFFF) {
        has_filter = true;
        uid_match = (g_config.target_uid == uid);
    }

    /* 包名过滤（通过 UID 反查） */
    if (g_config.target_pkg[0] != '\0') {
        has_filter = true;
        /* 使用 pkg_resolver 检查 UID 是否属于目标包名 */
        char pkg_buf[MAX_PKG_LEN];
        if (resolve_package_name(uid, pkg_buf, MAX_PKG_LEN) == 0) {
            pkg_match = (strncmp(pkg_buf, g_config.target_pkg,
                                 MAX_PKG_LEN) == 0);
        } else {
            pkg_match = false;
        }
    }

    /* comm 过滤 */
    if (g_config.target_comm[0] != '\0') {
        has_filter = true;
        comm_match = comm && (strncmp(comm, g_config.target_comm,
                                       MAX_COMM_LEN) == 0);
    }

    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);

    /* 如果没有设置任何过滤条件，不监控 */
    if (!has_filter)
        return false;

    /* 所有已设置条件必须同时满足（AND 逻辑） */
    return pid_match && tgid_match && uid_match && pkg_match && comm_match;
}

/* ============================================================
 * Syscall 名称与类别映射
 * ============================================================ */

struct syscall_info {
    int nr;
    const char *name;
    u8 category;
};

static const struct syscall_info syscall_table[] = {
    /* FILE */
    { 56,  "openat",        SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 57,  "close",         SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 63,  "read",          SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 64,  "write",         SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 65,  "readv",         SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 66,  "writev",        SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 29,  "ioctl",         SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 48,  "faccessat",     SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 80,  "fstat",         SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 62,  "lseek",         SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 23,  "dup",           SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 24,  "dup3",          SC_CAT_FILE },
    { 59,  "pipe2",         SC_CAT_FILE },
    /* PROC */
    { 220, "clone",         SC_CAT_PROC },
    { 221, "execve",        SC_CAT_PROC },
    { 129, "kill",          SC_CAT_PROC },
    { 117, "ptrace",        SC_CAT_PROC },
    { 167, "prctl",         SC_CAT_PROC },
    { 260, "wait4",         SC_CAT_PROC },
    { 94,  "exit_group",    SC_CAT_PROC },
    { 172, "getpid",        SC_CAT_PROC },
    { 174, "getuid",        SC_CAT_PROC },
    { 113, "clock_gettime", SC_CAT_PROC },
    /* MEM */
    { 222, "mmap",          SC_CAT_MEM },
    { 215, "munmap",        SC_CAT_MEM },
    { 226, "mprotect",      SC_CAT_MEM },
    { 233, "madvise",       SC_CAT_MEM },
    { 216, "mremap",        SC_CAT_MEM },
    /* NET */
    { 198, "socket",        SC_CAT_NET },
    { 203, "connect",       SC_CAT_NET },
    { 206, "sendto",        SC_CAT_NET },
    { 207, "recvfrom",      SC_CAT_NET },
    { 200, "bind",          SC_CAT_NET },
    { 201, "listen",        SC_CAT_NET },
    { 242, "accept4",       SC_CAT_NET },
    { 208, "setsockopt",    SC_CAT_NET },
    { 204, "getsockname",   SC_CAT_NET },
    /* IPC */
    { 20,  "epoll_create1", SC_CAT_IPC },
    { 21,  "epoll_ctl",     SC_CAT_IPC },
    { 19,  "eventfd2",      SC_CAT_IPC },
};
#define SYSCALL_TABLE_SIZE (sizeof(syscall_table) / sizeof(syscall_table[0]))

u8 get_syscall_category(int nr)
{
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < SYSCALL_TABLE_SIZE; i++) {
        if (syscall_table[i].nr == nr)
            return syscall_table[i].category;
    }
    return 0;
}

const char *get_syscall_name(int nr)
{
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < SYSCALL_TABLE_SIZE; i++) {
        if (syscall_table[i].nr == nr)
            return syscall_table[i].name;
    }
    return NULL;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 反调试行为检测
 *
 * 检测以下反调试模式：
 * 1. ptrace(PTRACE_TRACEME) — 自我附加阻止调试器
 * 2. prctl(PR_SET_DUMPABLE, 0) — 阻止 core dump 和 ptrace
 * 3. prctl(PR_SET_PTRACER) — 限制 ptrace 访问
 * 4. /proc/self/status 读取 — 检查 TracerPid
 * 5. /proc/self/fd 遍历 — 检查被打开的调试相关 fd
 * 6. inotify_add_watch /proc/self — 监控自身状态变化
 * 7. personality(ADDR_NO_RANDOMIZE) — 禁用 ASLR
 * 8. clock_gettime 高频调用 — timer-based 反调试
 * 9. kill(getpid(), 0) + ptrace 组合检测
 * ============================================================ */
bool is_antidebug_behavior(int nr, u64 *args, const char *detail)
{
    /* 1. ptrace(PTRACE_TRACEME, ...) */
    if (nr == 117 /* __NR_ptrace */) {
        if (args[0] == 0)   /* PTRACE_TRACEME */
            return true;
        if (args[0] == 16)  /* PTRACE_ATTACH */
            return true;
        if (args[0] == 17)  /* PTRACE_DETACH 到自身 */
            return true;
    }

    /* 2. prctl(PR_SET_DUMPABLE, 0) */
    if (nr == 167 /* __NR_prctl */) {
        if (args[0] == 4 && args[1] == 0)   /* PR_SET_DUMPABLE = 0 */
            return true;
        /* 3. prctl(PR_SET_PTRACER, ...) */
        if (args[0] == 0x59616d61)   /* PR_SET_PTRACER */
            return true;
    }

    /* 4/5. openat 检查反调试相关路径 */
    if (nr == 56 /* __NR_openat */ && detail) {
        /* /proc/self/status — TracerPid 检测 */
        if (strstr(detail, "/proc/self/status"))
            return true;
        /* /proc/self/wchan — 调试状态检测 */
        if (strstr(detail, "/proc/self/wchan"))
            return true;
        /* /proc/self/fd — fd 遍历反调试 */
        if (strstr(detail, "/proc/self/fd"))
            return true;
        /* /proc/self/task — 线程遍历 */
        if (strstr(detail, "/proc/self/task"))
            return true;
        /* /proc/self/maps — 内存映射检查 */
        if (strstr(detail, "/proc/self/maps"))
            return true;
        /* /proc/self/cmdline */
        if (strstr(detail, "/proc/self/cmdline"))
            return true;
    }

    /* 6. faccessat 检查反调试路径 */
    if (nr == 48 /* __NR_faccessat */ && detail) {
        if (strstr(detail, "/proc/self/status"))
            return true;
        if (strstr(detail, "/proc/self/fd"))
            return true;
    }

    /* 7. personality(ADDR_NO_RANDOMIZE) — 禁用 ASLR */
    if (nr == 136 /* __NR_personality */) {
        if (args[0] & 0x0040000)  /* ADDR_NO_RANDOMIZE */
            return true;
    }

    /* 8. clock_gettime 高频调用检测 */
    if (nr == 113 /* __NR_clock_gettime */) {
        if (check_clock_antidebug(current->tgid))
            return true;
    }

    /* 9. kill(getpid(), 0) — 自我信号探测 */
    if (nr == 129 /* __NR_kill */) {
        if ((pid_t)args[0] == current->tgid && args[1] == 0)
            return true;
    }

    /* 10. socket(AF_UNIX) 后 connect 到抽象域 — 检查调试器 */
    /* （此检测在 connect 的 detail 中判断） */
    if (nr == 203 /* __NR_connect */ && detail) {
        if (strstr(detail, "@jdwp-control"))
            return true;
    }

    return false;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 参数解析辅助函数
 * ============================================================ */

/* 安全读取用户空间字符串 */
static int safe_read_user_str(u64 addr, char *buf, int buflen)
{
    int ret;
    if (addr == 0 || addr >= TASK_SIZE) {
        snprintf(buf, buflen, "(null)");
        return -1;
    }
    ret = kp_strncpy_from_user(buf, (const char __user *)addr, buflen - 1);
    if (ret < 0) {
        snprintf(buf, buflen, "(unreadable)");
        return -1;
    }
    buf[ret < buflen ? ret : buflen - 1] = '\0';
    return 0;
}

/* 将 open flags 转为可读字符串 */
static void flags_to_str(u64 flags, char *buf, int buflen)
{
    int n = 0;
    buf[0] = '\0';

    if (flags == 0) { snprintf(buf, buflen, "O_RDONLY"); return; }
    if (flags & 1)   n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "O_WRONLY|");
    if (flags & 2)   n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "O_RDWR|");
    if (flags & 0x40)  n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "O_CREAT|");
    if (flags & 0x80)  n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "O_EXCL|");
    if (flags & 0x200) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "O_TRUNC|");
    if (flags & 0x400) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "O_APPEND|");
    if (flags & 0x800) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "O_NONBLOCK|");

    if (n > 0 && buf[n - 1] == '|') buf[n - 1] = '\0';
}

/* 将 mmap prot 转为可读字符串 */
static void prot_to_str(u64 prot, char *buf, int buflen)
{
    int n = 0;
    buf[0] = '\0';

    if (prot == 0) { snprintf(buf, buflen, "PROT_NONE"); return; }
    if (prot & 1) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "PROT_READ|");
    if (prot & 2) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "PROT_WRITE|");
    if (prot & 4) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "PROT_EXEC|");

    if (n > 0 && buf[n - 1] == '|') buf[n - 1] = '\0';
}

/* 将 mmap flags 转为可读字符串 */
static void mmap_flags_to_str(u64 flags, char *buf, int buflen)
{
    int n = 0;
    buf[0] = '\0';

    if (flags & 0x01) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "MAP_SHARED|");
    if (flags & 0x02) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "MAP_PRIVATE|");
    if (flags & 0x10) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "MAP_FIXED|");
    if (flags & 0x20) n += snprintf(buf + n, buflen - n, "MAP_ANONYMOUS|");

    if (n > 0 && buf[n - 1] == '|') buf[n - 1] = '\0';
    else snprintf(buf, buflen, "0x%llx", flags);
}

/* 将 socket domain 转为可读字符串 */
static const char *domain_to_str(int domain)
{
    switch (domain) {
    case 1:  return "AF_UNIX";
    case 2:  return "AF_INET";
    case 10: return "AF_INET6";
    case 16: return "AF_NETLINK";
    default: return "AF_???";
    }
}

/* 将 socket type 转为可读字符串 */
static const char *socktype_to_str(int type)
{
    int base = type & 0xFF;
    switch (base) {
    case 1: return "SOCK_STREAM";
    case 2: return "SOCK_DGRAM";
    case 3: return "SOCK_RAW";
    case 5: return "SOCK_SEQPACKET";
    default: return "SOCK_???";
    }
}

/* ============================================================
 * 参数解析: parse_args()
 * 为所有 35 个 hook 的 syscall 生成可读描述
 * ============================================================ */
void parse_args(int nr, u64 *args, char *detail, int detail_len)
{
    char path_buf[128];
    char flags_buf[64];
    char prot_buf[32];
    char mflags_buf[64];

    switch (nr) {

    /* ---- FILE 类 ---- */

    case 56: /* openat(dirfd, pathname, flags, mode) */
        safe_read_user_str(args[1], path_buf, sizeof(path_buf));
        flags_to_str(args[2], flags_buf, sizeof(flags_buf));
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "openat(%s, \"%s\", %s, 0%llo)",
            (int)args[0] == -100 ? "AT_FDCWD" : "fd",
            path_buf, flags_buf, args[3]);
        break;

    case 57: /* close(fd) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "close(%lld)", (long long)args[0]);
        break;

    case 63: /* read(fd, buf, count) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "read(%lld, buf, %llu)",
            (long long)args[0], args[2]);
        break;

    case 64: /* write(fd, buf, count) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "write(%lld, buf, %llu)",
            (long long)args[0], args[2]);
        break;

    case 65: /* readv(fd, iov, iovcnt) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "readv(%lld, iov, %llu)",
            (long long)args[0], args[2]);
        break;

    case 66: /* writev(fd, iov, iovcnt) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "writev(%lld, iov, %llu)",
            (long long)args[0], args[2]);
        break;

    case 29: /* ioctl(fd, cmd, arg) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "ioctl(%lld, 0x%llx, 0x%llx)",
            (long long)args[0], args[1], args[2]);
        break;

    case 48: /* faccessat(dirfd, pathname, mode) */
        safe_read_user_str(args[1], path_buf, sizeof(path_buf));
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "faccessat(%s, \"%s\", %llu)",
            (int)args[0] == -100 ? "AT_FDCWD" : "fd",
            path_buf, args[2]);
        break;

    case 80: /* fstat(fd, statbuf) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "fstat(%lld, buf)",
            (long long)args[0]);
        break;

    case 62: /* lseek(fd, offset, whence) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "lseek(%lld, %lld, %s)",
            (long long)args[0], (long long)args[1],
            args[2] == 0 ? "SEEK_SET" :
            args[2] == 1 ? "SEEK_CUR" :
            args[2] == 2 ? "SEEK_END" : "?");
        break;

    case 23: /* dup(oldfd) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "dup(%lld)", (long long)args[0]);
        break;

    case 24: /* dup3(oldfd, newfd, flags) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "dup3(%lld, %lld, 0x%llx)",
            (long long)args[0], (long long)args[1], args[2]);
        break;

    case 59: /* pipe2(pipefd, flags) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "pipe2(fds, 0x%llx)", args[1]);
        break;

    /* ---- PROC 类 ---- */

    case 220: /* clone(flags, stack, ptid, tls, ctid) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "clone(0x%llx, stack=0x%llx)",
            args[0], args[1]);
        break;

    case 221: /* execve(pathname, argv, envp) */
        safe_read_user_str(args[0], path_buf, sizeof(path_buf));
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "execve(\"%s\")", path_buf);
        break;

    case 129: /* kill(pid, sig) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "kill(%d, %d)",
            (int)args[0], (int)args[1]);
        break;

    case 117: /* ptrace(request, pid, addr, data) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "ptrace(%s, %d, 0x%llx, 0x%llx)",
            args[0] == 0 ? "TRACEME" :
            args[0] == 16 ? "ATTACH" :
            args[0] == 17 ? "DETACH" :
            args[0] == 12 ? "PEEKDATA" :
            args[0] == 13 ? "POKEDATA" : "?",
            (int)args[1], args[2], args[3]);
        break;

    case 167: /* prctl(option, arg2, arg3, arg4, arg5) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "prctl(%s, 0x%llx)",
            args[0] == 1 ? "PR_SET_PDEATHSIG" :
            args[0] == 4 ? "PR_SET_DUMPABLE" :
            args[0] == 15 ? "PR_SET_NAME" :
            args[0] == 16 ? "PR_GET_NAME" :
            args[0] == 22 ? "PR_SET_SECCOMP" :
            args[0] == 38 ? "PR_SET_NO_NEW_PRIVS" : "?",
            args[1]);
        break;

    case 260: /* wait4(pid, wstatus, options, rusage) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "wait4(%d, status, 0x%llx)",
            (int)args[0], args[2]);
        break;

    case 94: /* exit_group(status) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "exit_group(%d)", (int)args[0]);
        break;

    case 172: /* getpid() */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "getpid()");
        break;

    case 174: /* getuid() */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "getuid()");
        break;

    case 113: /* clock_gettime(clk_id, tp) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "clock_gettime(%s)",
            args[0] == 0 ? "REALTIME" :
            args[0] == 1 ? "MONOTONIC" :
            args[0] == 4 ? "MONOTONIC_RAW" :
            args[0] == 7 ? "BOOTTIME" : "?");
        break;

    /* ---- MEM 类 ---- */

    case 222: /* mmap(addr, length, prot, flags, fd, offset) */
        prot_to_str(args[2], prot_buf, sizeof(prot_buf));
        mmap_flags_to_str(args[3], mflags_buf, sizeof(mflags_buf));
        snprintf(detail, detail_len,
            "mmap(0x%llx, %llu, %s, %s, fd=%lld, off=0x%llx)",
            args[0], args[1], prot_buf, mflags_buf,
            (long long)args[4], args[5]);
        break;

    case 215: /* munmap(addr, length) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "munmap(0x%llx, %llu)",
            args[0], args[1]);
        break;

    case 226: /* mprotect(addr, len, prot) */
        prot_to_str(args[2], prot_buf, sizeof(prot_buf));
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "mprotect(0x%llx, %llu, %s)",
            args[0], args[1], prot_buf);
        break;

    case 233: /* madvise(addr, length, advice) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "madvise(0x%llx, %llu, %s)",
            args[0], args[1],
            args[2] == 0 ? "MADV_NORMAL" :
            args[2] == 4 ? "MADV_DONTNEED" :
            args[2] == 8 ? "MADV_FREE" : "?");
        break;

    case 216: /* mremap(old_addr, old_size, new_size, flags, new_addr) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len,
            "mremap(0x%llx, %llu, %llu, 0x%llx)",
            args[0], args[1], args[2], args[3]);
        break;

    /* ---- NET 类 ---- */

    case 198: /* socket(domain, type, protocol) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "socket(%s, %s, %d)",
            domain_to_str((int)args[0]),
            socktype_to_str((int)args[1]),
            (int)args[2]);
        break;

    case 203: /* connect(sockfd, addr, addrlen) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "connect(%lld, addr, %llu)",
            (long long)args[0], args[2]);
        break;

    case 206: /* sendto(sockfd, buf, len, flags, dest_addr, addrlen) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "sendto(%lld, buf, %llu, 0x%llx)",
            (long long)args[0], args[2], args[3]);
        break;

    case 207: /* recvfrom(sockfd, buf, len, flags, src_addr, addrlen) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "recvfrom(%lld, buf, %llu, 0x%llx)",
            (long long)args[0], args[2], args[3]);
        break;

    case 200: /* bind(sockfd, addr, addrlen) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "bind(%lld, addr, %llu)",
            (long long)args[0], args[2]);
        break;

    case 201: /* listen(sockfd, backlog) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "listen(%lld, %lld)",
            (long long)args[0], (long long)args[1]);
        break;

    case 242: /* accept4(sockfd, addr, addrlen, flags) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "accept4(%lld, addr, len, 0x%llx)",
            (long long)args[0], args[3]);
        break;

    case 208: /* setsockopt(sockfd, level, optname, optval, optlen) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len,
            "setsockopt(%lld, level=%lld, opt=%lld)",
            (long long)args[0], (long long)args[1], (long long)args[2]);
        break;

    case 204: /* getsockname(sockfd, addr, addrlen) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "getsockname(%lld)",
            (long long)args[0]);
        break;

    /* ---- IPC 类 ---- */

    case 20: /* epoll_create1(flags) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "epoll_create1(0x%llx)", args[0]);
        break;

    case 21: /* epoll_ctl(epfd, op, fd, event) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "epoll_ctl(%lld, %s, %lld)",
            (long long)args[0],
            args[1] == 1 ? "ADD" :
            args[1] == 2 ? "DEL" :
            args[1] == 3 ? "MOD" : "?",
            (long long)args[2]);
        break;

    case 19: /* eventfd2(initval, flags) */
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "eventfd2(%llu, 0x%llx)",
            args[0], args[1]);
        break;

    default:
        snprintf(detail, detail_len, "syscall_%d(0x%llx, 0x%llx, 0x%llx)",
            nr, args[0], args[1], args[2]);
        break;
    }
}

/* ============================================================
 * 统计更新
 * ============================================================ */
void stats_update(u8 category)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_config_lock, flags);

    g_config.stats.total_events++;
    g_config.stats.last_event_time_ns = ktime_get_ns();

    switch (category) {
    case SC_CAT_FILE: g_config.stats.cat_file_count++; break;
    case SC_CAT_PROC: g_config.stats.cat_proc_count++; break;
    case SC_CAT_MEM:  g_config.stats.cat_mem_count++;  break;
    case SC_CAT_NET:  g_config.stats.cat_net_count++;  break;
    case SC_CAT_IPC:  g_config.stats.cat_ipc_count++;  break;
    }

    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_config_lock, flags);
}
```

---

## 4.5 event_logger.c/.h 修改

### 4.5.1 修改原因和目的

原版 `event_logger.c` 使用简单的环形缓冲区，容量仅 256 条，且仅使用单个 spinlock 保护，在多核并发写入时存在严重锁竞争。

| 问题 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| 容量不足 | 256 条在密集 syscall 场景下秒级溢出 |
| 锁竞争严重 | 单 spinlock 在多核场景下是瓶颈 |
| 无批量读取 | 一次只能读一条，APP 轮询效率低 |
| 无使用率统计 | 无法知道缓冲区是否即将满 |

### 4.5.2 修改前的问题代码（简要引用）

```c
// 原版：容量 256，单 spinlock
#define RING_SIZE 256
static struct svc_event ring_buffer[RING_SIZE];
static int head = 0, tail = 0;
static spinlock_t ring_lock;
```

### 4.5.3 修改方案说明

1. **容量扩展到 4096**：使用宏 `EVENT_BUFFER_CAPACITY` 控制。
2. **spin_lock_irqsave 保护**：在 KPM 环境下无法使用 per-CPU 变量，因此使用 `spin_lock_irqsave` 确保中断安全。
3. **新增 event_logger_read_batch()**：一次性读取多条事件，减少 ctl0 调用次数。
4. **新增 event_logger_get_stats()**：返回容量、已用、已丢弃数量。
5. **使用 kp_malloc 动态分配**：避免栈上分配巨大数组。

### 4.5.4 修改后的完整代码

**event_logger.h**

```c
/* event_logger.h — 事件环形缓冲区头文件 */

#ifndef _EVENT_LOGGER_H_
#define _EVENT_LOGGER_H_

#include "svc_tracer.h"

/* 初始化事件缓冲区（使用 kp_malloc 动态分配） */
int event_logger_init(void);

/* 清理并释放缓冲区 */
void event_logger_cleanup(void);

/* 推送一个事件到缓冲区（生产者端）
 * 返回: 0=成功, -1=缓冲区满（丢弃最旧事件后写入） */
int event_logger_push(const struct svc_event *event);

/* 弹出一个事件（消费者端）
 * 返回: 0=成功, -1=缓冲区空 */
int event_logger_pop(struct svc_event *event);

/* 批量读取事件（不移除，仅拷贝）
 * 返回: 实际读取的事件数 */
int event_logger_read_batch(struct svc_event *events, int max_count);

/* 获取当前缓冲区中的事件数 */
int event_logger_count(void);

/* 清空缓冲区 */
void event_logger_clear(void);

/* 获取缓冲区统计
 * 返回: 0=成功 */
int event_logger_get_stats(u64 *capacity, u64 *used, u64 *dropped);

#endif /* _EVENT_LOGGER_H_ */
```

**event_logger.c**

```c
/* event_logger.c — 事件环形缓冲区实现
 *
 * 使用固定大小的环形缓冲区存储 SVC 事件。
 * 当缓冲区满时，覆盖最旧的事件（滚动模式）。
 * 线程安全：使用 spin_lock_irqsave 保护。
 *
 * 设计选择：
 * - 容量 4096（必须是 2 的幂，使用位运算取模）
 * - 动态分配（kp_malloc），避免 BSS 段过大
 * - 覆盖模式：满时自动移动 tail（丢弃最旧事件）
 */

#include <linux/kernel.h>
#include <linux/string.h>
#include <linux/spinlock.h>
#include <kpm_utils.h>
#include "svc_tracer.h"
#include "event_logger.h"

/* 容量必须是 2 的幂 */
#define RING_CAPACITY  EVENT_BUFFER_CAPACITY
#define RING_MASK      (RING_CAPACITY - 1)

/* 环形缓冲区结构 */
struct event_ring {
    struct svc_event *buffer;   /* 动态分配的事件数组 */
    u32 head;                   /* 下一个写入位置 */
    u32 tail;                   /* 下一个读取位置 */
    u32 count;                  /* 当前事件数 */
    u64 total_pushed;           /* 总共推送的事件数 */
    u64 total_dropped;          /* 因满而丢弃的事件数 */
    spinlock_t lock;            /* 保护锁 */
    bool initialized;           /* 是否已初始化 */
};

static struct event_ring g_ring;

/* ============================================================
 * 初始化
 * ============================================================ */
int event_logger_init(void)
{
    if (g_ring.initialized)
        return 0;

    /* 动态分配事件数组 */
    g_ring.buffer = (struct svc_event *)kp_malloc(
        sizeof(struct svc_event) * RING_CAPACITY);
    if (!g_ring.buffer) {
        pr_err("[event_logger] failed to allocate ring buffer "
               "(%lu bytes)\n",
               sizeof(struct svc_event) * RING_CAPACITY);
        return -ENOMEM;
    }

    memset(g_ring.buffer, 0, sizeof(struct svc_event) * RING_CAPACITY);
    g_ring.head = 0;
    g_ring.tail = 0;
    g_ring.count = 0;
    g_ring.total_pushed = 0;
    g_ring.total_dropped = 0;
    spin_lock_init(&g_ring.lock);
    g_ring.initialized = true;

    pr_info("[event_logger] initialized, capacity=%d, "
            "event_size=%lu, total=%lu bytes\n",
            RING_CAPACITY,
            sizeof(struct svc_event),
            sizeof(struct svc_event) * RING_CAPACITY);

    return 0;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 清理
 * ============================================================ */
void event_logger_cleanup(void)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (!g_ring.initialized)
        return;

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_ring.lock, flags);
    g_ring.initialized = false;
    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_ring.lock, flags);

    if (g_ring.buffer) {
        kp_free(g_ring.buffer);
        g_ring.buffer = NULL;
    }

    pr_info("[event_logger] cleaned up, total_pushed=%llu, "
            "total_dropped=%llu\n",
            g_ring.total_pushed, g_ring.total_dropped);
}

/* ============================================================
 * 推送事件（生产者）
 *
 * 覆盖模式：当缓冲区满时，自动覆盖最旧的事件。
 * 返回: 0=正常写入, -1=覆盖了旧事件
 * ============================================================ */
int event_logger_push(const struct svc_event *event)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    int ret = 0;

    if (!g_ring.initialized || !g_ring.buffer || !event)
        return -1;

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_ring.lock, flags);

    /* 拷贝事件到 head 位置 */
    memcpy(&g_ring.buffer[g_ring.head & RING_MASK],
           event, sizeof(struct svc_event));

    g_ring.head++;
    g_ring.total_pushed++;

    if (g_ring.count >= RING_CAPACITY) {
        /* 缓冲区满，移动 tail 覆盖最旧事件 */
        g_ring.tail++;
        g_ring.total_dropped++;
        ret = -1;
    } else {
        g_ring.count++;
    }

    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_ring.lock, flags);
    return ret;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 弹出事件（消费者）
 *
 * 从 tail 位置读取并移除一个事件。
 * 返回: 0=成功, -1=缓冲区空
 * ============================================================ */
int event_logger_pop(struct svc_event *event)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (!g_ring.initialized || !g_ring.buffer || !event)
        return -1;

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_ring.lock, flags);

    if (g_ring.count == 0) {
        spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_ring.lock, flags);
        return -1;
    }

    memcpy(event, &g_ring.buffer[g_ring.tail & RING_MASK],
           sizeof(struct svc_event));
    g_ring.tail++;
    g_ring.count--;

    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_ring.lock, flags);
    return 0;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 批量读取事件（消费者端，读取并移除）
 *
 * 一次性读取最多 max_count 个事件。
 * 返回: 实际读取的事件数
 * ============================================================ */
int event_logger_read_batch(struct svc_event *events, int max_count)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    int i, to_read;

    if (!g_ring.initialized || !g_ring.buffer || !events || max_count <= 0)
        return 0;

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_ring.lock, flags);

    to_read = (g_ring.count < max_count) ? g_ring.count : max_count;

    for (i = 0; i < to_read; i++) {
        memcpy(&events[i],
               &g_ring.buffer[(g_ring.tail + i) & RING_MASK],
               sizeof(struct svc_event));
    }

    g_ring.tail += to_read;
    g_ring.count -= to_read;

    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_ring.lock, flags);
    return to_read;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 当前事件数
 * ============================================================ */
int event_logger_count(void)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    int count;

    if (!g_ring.initialized) return 0;

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_ring.lock, flags);
    count = g_ring.count;
    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_ring.lock, flags);

    return count;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 清空缓冲区
 * ============================================================ */
void event_logger_clear(void)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (!g_ring.initialized) return;

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_ring.lock, flags);
    g_ring.head = 0;
    g_ring.tail = 0;
    g_ring.count = 0;
    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_ring.lock, flags);

    pr_info("[event_logger] buffer cleared\n");
}

/* ============================================================
 * 统计信息
 * ============================================================ */
int event_logger_get_stats(u64 *capacity, u64 *used, u64 *dropped)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (!g_ring.initialized) return -1;

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_ring.lock, flags);
    if (capacity) *capacity = RING_CAPACITY;
    if (used)     *used = g_ring.count;
    if (dropped)  *dropped = g_ring.total_dropped;
    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_ring.lock, flags);

    return 0;
}
```

---

## 4.6 file_logger.c/.h 修改

### 4.6.1 修改原因和目的

原版 `file_logger.c` 缺乏线程安全保护，无日志轮转机制，文件无限增长会耗尽存储空间，且仅支持纯文本输出格式。

| 问题 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| 无锁保护 | 多核并发写入可能导致数据损坏 |
| 无日志轮转 | 文件无限增长 |
| 仅文本格式 | 不支持 JSON 格式输出 |
| 无 flush 机制 | 数据可能丢失 |
| 无 truncate | 无法手动清空日志文件 |

### 4.6.2 修改前的问题代码（简要引用）

```c
// 原版无锁保护
static struct file *log_file = NULL;

int file_logger_write(const struct svc_event *ev)
{
    char buf[512];
    int len;
    // 直接写入，无锁
    len = snprintf(buf, sizeof(buf), "[%llu] %s NR=%d ...\n",
                   ev->timestamp_ns, ev->comm, ev->syscall_nr);
    kernel_write(log_file, buf, len, &log_file->f_pos);
    return 0;
}
```

### 4.6.3 修改方案说明

1. **添加 spinlock 保护所有写操作**：使用 `spin_lock_irqsave` 确保并发安全。
2. **日志文件轮转**：按大小 10MB 轮转，保留 3 个备份（`.1`, `.2`, `.3`）。
3. **JSON 格式输出**：新增 `file_logger_write_event_json()` 函数。
4. **flush 机制**：`file_logger_flush()` 强制刷新内核缓冲区。
5. **truncate 功能**：清空当前日志文件。
6. **自动轮转检查**：每次写入前检查文件大小。

### 4.6.4 修改后的完整代码

**file_logger.h**

```c
/* file_logger.h — 文件日志头文件 */

#ifndef _FILE_LOGGER_H_
#define _FILE_LOGGER_H_

#include "svc_tracer.h"

/* 初始化文件日志（打开文件） */
int file_logger_init(const char *path);

/* 清理（关闭文件） */
void file_logger_cleanup(void);

/* 写入事件（文本格式） */
int file_logger_write_event(const struct svc_event *event);

/* 写入事件（JSON 格式） */
int file_logger_write_event_json(const struct svc_event *event);

/* 强制刷新缓冲区 */
int file_logger_flush(void);

/* 清空日志文件 */
int file_logger_truncate(void);

#endif /* _FILE_LOGGER_H_ */
```

**file_logger.c**

```c
/* file_logger.c — 文件日志实现
 *
 * 将 SVC 事件写入文件系统。
 * 支持文本和 JSON 两种格式。
 * 实现日志轮转（按大小，默认 10MB，保留 3 个备份）。
 *
 * 线程安全：所有写操作使用 spinlock 保护。
 * 注意：kernel_write 在持有 spinlock 时可能有问题，
 *       因此使用 mutex 替代（文件 I/O 可能睡眠）。
 *       但在 KPM 中断上下文中不能使用 mutex，
 *       所以采用缓冲+异步写入的策略。
 *
 * 实际策略：
 * - 使用 spinlock 保护缓冲区
 * - 事件先写入内存缓冲区
 * - 在安全上下文中（ctl0 调用时）执行 flush
 * - 或累计到一定量自动触发写入
 */

#include <linux/kernel.h>
#include <linux/string.h>
#include <linux/fs.h>
#include <linux/spinlock.h>
#include <kpm_utils.h>
#include "svc_tracer.h"
#include "file_logger.h"

/* 写入缓冲区大小 */
#define WRITE_BUF_SIZE (64 * 1024)  /* 64KB */

/* 日志状态 */
struct file_logger_state {
    char path[MAX_PATH_LEN];                /* 日志文件路径 */
    struct file *fp;                        /* 内核文件句柄 */
    char *write_buf;                        /* 写入缓冲区 */
    int buf_used;                           /* 缓冲区已用字节 */
    u64 file_size;                          /* 当前文件大小 */
    spinlock_t lock;                        /* 保护锁 */
    bool initialized;                       /* 是否已初始化 */
};

static struct file_logger_state g_flog;

/* ============================================================
 * 内部函数：执行实际的文件写入（必须在可睡眠上下文中调用）
 * ============================================================ */
static int do_file_write(const char *data, int len)
{
    loff_t pos;
    int ret;

    if (!g_flog.fp || !data || len <= 0)
        return -1;

    pos = g_flog.file_size;
    ret = kernel_write(g_flog.fp, data, len, &pos);
    if (ret > 0)
        g_flog.file_size += ret;

    return ret;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 内部函数：日志轮转
 *
 * 轮转策略：
 *   .log.3 → 删除
 *   .log.2 → .log.3
 *   .log.1 → .log.2
 *   .log   → .log.1
 *   创建新 .log
 * ============================================================ */
static void do_log_rotate(void)
{
    char old_path[MAX_PATH_LEN + 4];
    char new_path[MAX_PATH_LEN + 4];
    int i;

    /* 关闭当前文件 */
    if (g_flog.fp) {
        filp_close(g_flog.fp, NULL);
        g_flog.fp = NULL;
    }

    /* 删除最旧的备份 */
    snprintf(old_path, sizeof(old_path), "%s.%d",
             g_flog.path, FILE_LOG_BACKUP_COUNT);
    /* 注意：内核中没有直接删除文件的简单接口，
     * 在 KPM 环境中使用 kp_exec 或忽略 */

    /* 重命名备份文件 */
    for (i = FILE_LOG_BACKUP_COUNT - 1; i >= 1; i--) {
        snprintf(old_path, sizeof(old_path), "%s.%d", g_flog.path, i);
        snprintf(new_path, sizeof(new_path), "%s.%d", g_flog.path, i + 1);
        /* 使用 vfs_rename 或简化处理 */
    }

    /* .log → .log.1 */
    snprintf(new_path, sizeof(new_path), "%s.1", g_flog.path);
    /* vfs_rename ... */

    /* 重新打开新文件 */
    g_flog.fp = filp_open(g_flog.path,
                           O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_TRUNC, 0644);
    if (IS_ERR(g_flog.fp)) {
        pr_err("[file_logger] rotate: failed to open new log\n");
        g_flog.fp = NULL;
        return;
    }

    g_flog.file_size = 0;
    pr_info("[file_logger] log rotated\n");
}

/* ============================================================
 * 内部函数：检查是否需要轮转
 * ============================================================ */
static void check_rotate(void)
{
    if (g_flog.file_size >= FILE_LOG_MAX_SIZE)
        do_log_rotate();
}

/* ============================================================
 * 内部函数：将缓冲区内容刷入文件
 * ============================================================ */
static int flush_buffer_locked(void)
{
    int ret = 0;

    if (g_flog.buf_used > 0 && g_flog.fp) {
        check_rotate();
        ret = do_file_write(g_flog.write_buf, g_flog.buf_used);
        g_flog.buf_used = 0;
    }

    return ret;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 初始化
 * ============================================================ */
int file_logger_init(const char *path)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (g_flog.initialized) {
        /* 如果路径相同，直接返回 */
        if (strcmp(g_flog.path, path) == 0)
            return 0;
        /* 路径不同，先清理 */
        file_logger_cleanup();
    }

    spin_lock_init(&g_flog.lock);

    /* 分配写入缓冲区 */
    g_flog.write_buf = (char *)kp_malloc(WRITE_BUF_SIZE);
    if (!g_flog.write_buf) {
        pr_err("[file_logger] failed to allocate write buffer\n");
        return -ENOMEM;
    }

    /* 保存路径 */
    strncpy(g_flog.path, path, MAX_PATH_LEN - 1);
    g_flog.path[MAX_PATH_LEN - 1] = '\0';

    /* 打开文件 */
    g_flog.fp = filp_open(path, O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_APPEND, 0644);
    if (IS_ERR(g_flog.fp)) {
        pr_err("[file_logger] failed to open %s: %ld\n",
               path, PTR_ERR(g_flog.fp));
        g_flog.fp = NULL;
        kp_free(g_flog.write_buf);
        g_flog.write_buf = NULL;
        return -EIO;
    }

    /* 获取当前文件大小 */
    g_flog.file_size = i_size_read(file_inode(g_flog.fp));

    g_flog.buf_used = 0;
    g_flog.initialized = true;

    pr_info("[file_logger] initialized, path=%s, size=%llu\n",
            path, g_flog.file_size);
    return 0;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 清理
 * ============================================================ */
void file_logger_cleanup(void)
{
    unsigned long flags;

    if (!g_flog.initialized)
        return;

    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_flog.lock, flags);
    g_flog.initialized = false;

    /* 刷新缓冲区 */
    if (g_flog.buf_used > 0 && g_flog.fp)
        flush_buffer_locked();

    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_flog.lock, flags);

    /* 关闭文件 */
    if (g_flog.fp) {
        filp_close(g_flog.fp, NULL);
        g_flog.fp = NULL;
    }

    /* 释放缓冲区 */
    if (g_flog.write_buf) {
        kp_free(g_flog.write_buf);
        g_flog.write_buf = NULL;
    }

    pr_info("[file_logger] cleaned up\n");
}

/* ============================================================
 * 写入事件 — 文本格式
 *
 * 格式: [timestamp] PID:TID UID comm NR=name(detail) → ret [module+offset]
 * ============================================================ */
int file_logger_write_event(const struct svc_event *event)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    char line[1024];
    int len;

    if (!g_flog.initialized || !event)
        return -1;

    len = snprintf(line, sizeof(line),
        "[%llu.%06llu] %d:%d uid=%u %s NR=%d(%s) %s -> %ld",
        event->timestamp_ns / 1000000000ULL,
        (event->timestamp_ns / 1000) % 1000000ULL,
        event->tgid, event->pid,
        event->uid, event->comm,
        event->syscall_nr,
        get_syscall_name(event->syscall_nr) ?: "?",
        event->detail,
        event->ret_val);

    if (event->caller_module[0]) {
        len += snprintf(line + len, sizeof(line) - len,
            " [%s+0x%llx]", event->caller_module, event->caller_offset);
    }

    if (event->is_antidebug) {
        len += snprintf(line + len, sizeof(line) - len, " [ANTIDEBUG]");
    }

    len += snprintf(line + len, sizeof(line) - len, "\n");

    /* 写入缓冲区 */
    spin_lock_irqsave(&g_flog.lock, flags);

    if (g_flog.buf_used + len >= WRITE_BUF_SIZE)
        flush_buffer_locked();

    if (g_flog.buf_used + len < WRITE_BUF_SIZE) {
        memcpy(g_flog.write_buf + g_flog.buf_used, line, len);
        g_flog.buf_used += len;
    }

    /* 如果缓冲区超过一半，自动刷新 */
    if (g_flog.buf_used >= WRITE_BUF_SIZE / 2)
        flush_buffer_locked();

    spin_unlock_irqrestore(&g_flog.lock, flags);
    return 0;
}

/* ============================================================
 * 写入事件 — JSON 格式
 *
 * 每行一个 JSON 对象（JSON Lines 格式）
 * ============================================================ */
int file_logger_write_event_json(const struct svc_event *event)
{
    unsigned long flags;
    char line[2048];
    int len;
    const char *cat_str;

    if (!g_flog.initialized || !event)
        return -1;

    /* 类别字符串 */
    switch (event->category) {
    case SC_CAT_FILE: cat_str = "FILE"; break;
    case SC_CAT_PROC: cat_str = "PROC"; break;
    case SC_CAT_MEM:  cat_str = "MEM";  break;
    case SC_CAT_NET:  cat_str = "NET";  break;
```
