```kotlin
        val kpmAvailable = try {
            shellExecutor.execute("which kpatch-android", useSu = true)
            true
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            false
        }

        if (!kpmAvailable) {
            return EnvironmentStatus(
                rootAvailable = true,
                kpmAvailable = false,
                superKeyConfigured = hasSuperKey(),
                errorMessage = "kpatch-android 命令不可用，请确认 APatch/KernelPatch 已正确安装"
            )
        }

        return EnvironmentStatus(
            rootAvailable = true,
            kpmAvailable = true,
            superKeyConfigured = hasSuperKey(),
            errorMessage = if (!hasSuperKey()) "请输入 APatch SuperKey" else null
        )
    }

    // ==================== ctl0 命令执行 ====================

    /**
     * 执行 ctl0 命令并返回原始字符串输出
     *
     * @param command ctl0 命令（如 "status", "start", "get_events 50"）
     * @return 命令输出的原始 JSON 字符串
     */
    private suspend fun executeCtl0(command: String): String {
        val superKey = getSuperKey()
            ?: throw IllegalStateException("SuperKey not configured")

        // 构造完整命令：kpatch-android <SuperKey> kpm ctl0 svc-tracer '<command>'
        val fullCommand =
            "kpatch-android $superKey kpm ctl0 $KPM_MODULE_NAME '$command'"

        Log.d(TAG, "ctl0 command: $command")

        return try {
            val output = shellExecutor.execute(fullCommand)
            Log.d(TAG, "ctl0 response (${output.length} chars)")
            output
        } catch (e: ShellException) {
            Log.e(TAG, "ctl0 command failed: $command", e)
            throw KpmException("ctl0 command failed: ${e.message}", e)
        }
    }

    /**
     * 执行 ctl0 命令并解析 JSON 为指定类型
     */
    private suspend inline fun <reified T> executeCtl0Typed(command: String): T {
        val json = executeCtl0(command)
        return try {
            gson.fromJson(json, T::class.java)
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            Log.e(TAG, "JSON parse error for command '$command': $json", e)
            throw KpmException("Failed to parse response: ${e.message}", e)
        }
    }

    // ==================== 高层 API ====================

    /**
     * 获取模块运行状态
     */
    suspend fun getStatus(): TracerStatus {
        return executeCtl0Typed("status")
    }

    /**
     * 启动追踪器
     */
    suspend fun startTracer(): Boolean {
        val output = executeCtl0("start")
        return output.contains("ok", ignoreCase = true) ||
                output.contains("started", ignoreCase = true) ||
                output.contains("true", ignoreCase = true)
    }

    /**
     * 停止追踪器
     */
    suspend fun stopTracer(): Boolean {
        val output = executeCtl0("stop")
        return output.contains("ok", ignoreCase = true) ||
                output.contains("stopped", ignoreCase = true) ||
                output.contains("true", ignoreCase = true)
    }

    /**
     * 获取捕获的事件列表
     *
     * @param limit 获取的最大事件数量
     */
    suspend fun getEvents(limit: Int = 50): List<SvcEvent> {
        val json = executeCtl0("get_events $limit")
        return try {
            val type = object : TypeToken<List<SvcEvent>>() {}.type
            gson.fromJson(json, type) ?: emptyList()
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            Log.e(TAG, "Failed to parse events", e)
            throw KpmException("Failed to parse events: ${e.message}", e)
        }
    }

    /**
     * 获取当前追踪配置
     */
    suspend fun getConfig(): TracerConfig {
        return executeCtl0Typed("get_config")
    }

    /**
     * 设置追踪配置
     *
     * @param config 新的配置对象
     */
    suspend fun setConfig(config: TracerConfig): Boolean {
        val configJson = gson.toJson(config)
        // 需要对 JSON 中的单引号进行转义，因为外层使用单引号包裹
        val escapedJson = configJson.replace("'", "'\\''")
        val output = executeCtl0("set_config $escapedJson")
        return output.contains("ok", ignoreCase = true) ||
                output.contains("true", ignoreCase = true)
    }

    /**
     * 清空事件缓冲区
     */
    suspend fun clearEvents(): Boolean {
        val output = executeCtl0("clear_events")
        return output.contains("ok", ignoreCase = true) ||
                output.contains("true", ignoreCase = true)
    }

    /**
     * 获取统计数据
     */
    suspend fun getStats(): TracerStats {
        return executeCtl0Typed("get_stats")
    }

    // ==================== 辅助方法 ====================

    /**
     * 获取设备上已安装的应用列表（用于配置页面选择目标应用）
     *
     * @param includeSystem 是否包含系统应用
     * @return (包名, UID, 应用名) 三元组列表
     */
    fun getInstalledApps(includeSystem: Boolean = false): List<Triple<String, Int, String>> {
        val pm = context.packageManager
        val flags = if (includeSystem) {
            PackageManager.GET_META_DATA
        } else {
            PackageManager.GET_META_DATA
        }

        return pm.getInstalledApplications(flags)
            .filter { appInfo ->
                if (includeSystem) true
                else (appInfo.flags and android.content.pm.ApplicationInfo.FLAG_SYSTEM) == 0
            }
            .map { appInfo ->
                Triple(
                    appInfo.packageName,
                    appInfo.uid,
                    pm.getApplicationLabel(appInfo).toString()
                )
            }
            .sortedBy { it.third }
    }
}

/**
 * KPM 通信异常
 */
class KpmException(message: String, cause: Throwable? = null) : Exception(message, cause)

/**
 * 环境状态数据类
 */
data class EnvironmentStatus(
    val rootAvailable: Boolean,
    val kpmAvailable: Boolean,
    val superKeyConfigured: Boolean,
    val errorMessage: String? = null
) {
    val isReady: Boolean
        get() = rootAvailable && kpmAvailable && superKeyConfigured
}
```

### 6.5.4 SvcTracerRepository.kt — 数据仓库层

```kotlin
package com.svctracer.manager.domain

import android.util.Log
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.SvcEvent
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.TracerConfig
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.TracerStats
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.TracerStatus
import com.svctracer.manager.data.service.EnvironmentStatus
import com.svctracer.manager.data.service.KpmBridgeService
import kotlinx.coroutines.delay
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.Flow
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.flow
import javax.inject.Inject
import javax.inject.Singleton

/**
 * SVC Tracer 数据仓库
 *
 * 职责：
 * - 封装 KpmBridgeService 的底层调用
 * - 提供 Flow 形式的轮询数据流
 * - 统一错误处理，返回 Result 类型
 * - 作为 ViewModel 与 Service 之间的抽象层
 */
@Singleton
class SvcTracerRepository @Inject constructor(
    private val bridgeService: KpmBridgeService
) {
    companion object {
        private const val TAG = "SvcTracerRepository"
        private const val DEFAULT_POLL_INTERVAL_MS = 2000L
        private const val EVENTS_POLL_INTERVAL_MS = 1500L
        private const val STATS_POLL_INTERVAL_MS = 5000L
    }

    // ==================== SuperKey 管理代理 ====================

    fun saveSuperKey(key: String) = bridgeService.saveSuperKey(key)
    fun getSuperKey(): String? = bridgeService.getSuperKey()
    fun clearSuperKey() = bridgeService.clearSuperKey()
    fun hasSuperKey(): Boolean = bridgeService.hasSuperKey()

    // ==================== 环境检测 ====================

    suspend fun checkEnvironment(): Result<EnvironmentStatus> = runCatching {
        bridgeService.checkEnvironment()
    }

    // ==================== 单次操作 ====================

    suspend fun getStatus(): Result<TracerStatus> = runCatching {
        bridgeService.getStatus()
    }

    suspend fun startTracer(): Result<Boolean> = runCatching {
        bridgeService.startTracer()
    }

    suspend fun stopTracer(): Result<Boolean> = runCatching {
        bridgeService.stopTracer()
    }

    suspend fun getEvents(limit: Int = 50): Result<List<SvcEvent>> = runCatching {
        bridgeService.getEvents(limit)
    }

    suspend fun getConfig(): Result<TracerConfig> = runCatching {
        bridgeService.getConfig()
    }

    suspend fun setConfig(config: TracerConfig): Result<Boolean> = runCatching {
        bridgeService.setConfig(config)
    }

    suspend fun clearEvents(): Result<Boolean> = runCatching {
        bridgeService.clearEvents()
    }

    suspend fun getStats(): Result<TracerStats> = runCatching {
        bridgeService.getStats()
    }

    // ==================== 轮询 Flow ====================

    /**
     * 状态轮询 Flow
     * 每隔 intervalMs 毫秒获取一次模块状态
     */
    fun pollStatus(intervalMs: Long = DEFAULT_POLL_INTERVAL_MS): Flow<Result<TracerStatus>> = flow {
        while (true) {
            val result = getStatus()
            emit(result)
            result.onFailure {
                Log.w(TAG, "Status poll failed: ${it.message}")
            }
            delay(intervalMs)
        }
    }

    /**
     * 事件轮询 Flow
     * 每隔 intervalMs 毫秒获取一次最新事件
     */
    fun pollEvents(
        limit: Int = 50,
        intervalMs: Long = EVENTS_POLL_INTERVAL_MS
    ): Flow<Result<List<SvcEvent>>> = flow {
        while (true) {
            val result = getEvents(limit)
            emit(result)
            result.onFailure {
                Log.w(TAG, "Events poll failed: ${it.message}")
            }
            delay(intervalMs)
        }
    }

    /**
     * 统计数据轮询 Flow
     */
    fun pollStats(intervalMs: Long = STATS_POLL_INTERVAL_MS): Flow<Result<TracerStats>> = flow {
        while (true) {
            val result = getStats()
            emit(result)
            result.onFailure {
                Log.w(TAG, "Stats poll failed: ${it.message}")
            }
            delay(intervalMs)
        }
    }

    // ==================== 应用列表 ====================

    /**
     * 获取已安装应用列表
     */
    fun getInstalledApps(includeSystem: Boolean = false) =
        bridgeService.getInstalledApps(includeSystem)
}
```

### 6.5.5 Hilt 依赖注入配置

**AppModule.kt — Hilt DI 模块**

```kotlin
package com.svctracer.manager.di

import android.content.Context
import com.svctracer.manager.data.service.KpmBridgeService
import com.svctracer.manager.data.shell.RootShellExecutor
import com.svctracer.manager.domain.SvcTracerRepository
import dagger.Module
import dagger.Provides
import dagger.hilt.InstallIn
import dagger.hilt.android.qualifiers.ApplicationContext
import dagger.hilt.components.SingletonComponent
import javax.inject.Singleton

/**
 * Hilt 依赖注入模块
 *
 * 提供应用全局的单例依赖：
 * - RootShellExecutor: Root Shell 执行器
 * - KpmBridgeService: KPM 通信桥接服务
 * - SvcTracerRepository: 数据仓库
 *
 * 所有依赖安装在 SingletonComponent 中，生命周期与 Application 一致。
 * 注意：由于 RootShellExecutor、KpmBridgeService、SvcTracerRepository 
 * 都使用了 @Singleton @Inject constructor，Hilt 可以自动提供它们。
 * 此 Module 主要用于提供需要额外配置的依赖或第三方库依赖。
 */
@Module
@InstallIn(SingletonComponent::class)
object AppModule {

    /**
     * 如果需要自定义 RootShellExecutor 的配置，可以在这里提供。
     * 当前版本使用 @Inject constructor 自动注入，此方法作为扩展点保留。
     */
    // @Provides
    // @Singleton
    // fun provideRootShellExecutor(): RootShellExecutor = RootShellExecutor()
}
```

**SvcTracerApp.kt — Application 类**

```kotlin
package com.svctracer.manager

import android.app.Application
import dagger.hilt.android.HiltAndroidApp

/**
 * 应用 Application 类
 *
 * @HiltAndroidApp 注解触发 Hilt 代码生成，作为依赖注入的根组件。
 * 所有使用 @AndroidEntryPoint 的 Activity/Fragment 都依赖此 Application。
 */
@HiltAndroidApp
class SvcTracerApp : Application() {
    override fun onCreate() {
        super.onCreate()
        // 应用级初始化可以放在这里
        // 例如：日志框架初始化、全局异常处理等
    }
}
```

### 6.5.6 MainViewModel.kt — 主 ViewModel

```kotlin
package com.svctracer.manager.ui

import android.util.Log
import androidx.lifecycle.ViewModel
import androidx.lifecycle.viewModelScope
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.SvcEvent
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.TracerConfig
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.TracerStats
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.TracerStatus
import com.svctracer.manager.data.service.EnvironmentStatus
import com.svctracer.manager.domain.SvcTracerRepository
import dagger.hilt.android.lifecycle.HiltViewModel
import kotlinx.coroutines.Job
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.MutableStateFlow
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.StateFlow
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.asStateFlow
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.catch
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
import javax.inject.Inject

/**
 * 主 ViewModel — 应用的核心状态管理器
 *
 * 职责：
 * - 管理所有 UI 状态（通过 StateFlow 暴露给 Compose）
 * - 处理用户事件（连接、启动、停止、配置等）
 * - 管理轮询协程的生命周期
 * - 错误处理与用户通知
 *
 * 使用 @HiltViewModel 注解，由 Hilt 自动注入 Repository 依赖。
 */
@HiltViewModel
class MainViewModel @Inject constructor(
    private val repository: SvcTracerRepository
) : ViewModel() {

    companion object {
        private const val TAG = "MainViewModel"
    }

    // ==================== UI 状态 ====================

    /** 环境状态 */
    private val _environmentStatus = MutableStateFlow<EnvironmentStatus?>(null)
    val environmentStatus: StateFlow<EnvironmentStatus?> = _environmentStatus.asStateFlow()

    /** 模块运行状态 */
    private val _status = MutableStateFlow(TracerStatus())
    val status: StateFlow<TracerStatus> = _status.asStateFlow()

    /** 当前配置 */
    private val _config = MutableStateFlow(TracerConfig())
    val config: StateFlow<TracerConfig> = _config.asStateFlow()

    /** 事件列表 */
    private val _events = MutableStateFlow<List<SvcEvent>>(emptyList())
    val events: StateFlow<List<SvcEvent>> = _events.asStateFlow()

    /** 统计数据 */
    private val _stats = MutableStateFlow(TracerStats())
    val stats: StateFlow<TracerStats> = _stats.asStateFlow()

    /** 是否已连接（SuperKey 验证通过且环境就绪） */
    private val _isConnected = MutableStateFlow(false)
    val isConnected: StateFlow<Boolean> = _isConnected.asStateFlow()

    /** 加载状态 */
    private val _isLoading = MutableStateFlow(false)
    val isLoading: StateFlow<Boolean> = _isLoading.asStateFlow()

    /** 错误消息（用于 Snackbar 显示） */
    private val _errorMessage = MutableStateFlow<String?>(null)
    val errorMessage: StateFlow<String?> = _errorMessage.asStateFlow()

    /** 成功消息 */
    private val _successMessage = MutableStateFlow<String?>(null)
    val successMessage: StateFlow<String?> = _successMessage.asStateFlow()

    /** SuperKey 输入值 */
    private val _superKeyInput = MutableStateFlow("")
    val superKeyInput: StateFlow<String> = _superKeyInput.asStateFlow()

    /** 已安装应用列表缓存 */
    private val _installedApps = MutableStateFlow<List<Triple<String, Int, String>>>(emptyList())
    val installedApps: StateFlow<List<Triple<String, Int, String>>> = _installedApps.asStateFlow()

    /** 选中的目标包名 */
    private val _selectedPackages = MutableStateFlow<Set<String>>(emptySet())
    val selectedPackages: StateFlow<Set<String>> = _selectedPackages.asStateFlow()

    // ==================== 轮询 Job 管理 ====================

    private var statusPollJob: Job? = null
    private var eventsPollJob: Job? = null
    private var statsPollJob: Job? = null

    // ==================== 初始化 ====================

    init {
        // 检查是否已有保存的 SuperKey
        val savedKey = repository.getSuperKey()
        if (savedKey != null) {
            _superKeyInput.value = savedKey
            // 自动尝试连接
            connect()
        }
    }

    // ==================== 用户操作处理 ====================

    /**
     * 更新 SuperKey 输入
     */
    fun updateSuperKeyInput(value: String) {
        _superKeyInput.value = value
    }

    /**
     * 连接（验证环境 + 保存 SuperKey）
     */
    fun connect() {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            _isLoading.value = true
            _errorMessage.value = null

            try {
                val key = _superKeyInput.value.trim()
                if (key.isBlank()) {
                    _errorMessage.value = "请输入 SuperKey"
                    return@launch
                }

                // 保存 SuperKey
                repository.saveSuperKey(key)

                // 检测环境
                val envResult = repository.checkEnvironment()
                envResult.onSuccess { envStatus ->
                    _environmentStatus.value = envStatus
                    if (envStatus.isReady) {
                        _isConnected.value = true
                        _successMessage.value = "连接成功"
                        // 开始轮询
                        startPolling()
                        // 加载初始数据
                        loadInitialData()
                    } else {
                        _errorMessage.value = envStatus.errorMessage ?: "环境检测失败"
                    }
                }.onFailure { e ->
                    _errorMessage.value = "环境检测异常: ${e.message}"
                    Log.e(TAG, "Environment check failed", e)
                }
            } finally {
                _isLoading.value = false
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 断开连接
     */
    fun disconnect() {
        stopPolling()
        _isConnected.value = false
        _status.value = TracerStatus()
        _events.value = emptyList()
        _stats.value = TracerStats()
        repository.clearSuperKey()
        _superKeyInput.value = ""
        _successMessage.value = "已断开连接"
    }

    /**
     * 启动追踪器
     */
    fun startTracer() {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            _isLoading.value = true
            repository.startTracer()
                .onSuccess {
                    _successMessage.value = "追踪器已启动"
                    // 立即刷新状态
                    refreshStatus()
                }
                .onFailure { e ->
                    _errorMessage.value = "启动失败: ${e.message}"
                    Log.e(TAG, "Start tracer failed", e)
                }
            _isLoading.value = false
        }
    }

    /**
     * 停止追踪器
     */
    fun stopTracer() {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            _isLoading.value = true
            repository.stopTracer()
                .onSuccess {
                    _successMessage.value = "追踪器已停止"
                    refreshStatus()
                }
                .onFailure { e ->
                    _errorMessage.value = "停止失败: ${e.message}"
                    Log.e(TAG, "Stop tracer failed", e)
                }
            _isLoading.value = false
        }
    }

    /**
     * 应用配置
     */
    fun applyConfig(config: TracerConfig) {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            _isLoading.value = true
            repository.setConfig(config)
                .onSuccess {
                    _config.value = config
                    _successMessage.value = "配置已应用"
                }
                .onFailure { e ->
                    _errorMessage.value = "配置应用失败: ${e.message}"
                    Log.e(TAG, "Set config failed", e)
                }
            _isLoading.value = false
        }
    }

    /**
     * 清空事件
     */
    fun clearEvents() {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            repository.clearEvents()
                .onSuccess {
                    _events.value = emptyList()
                    _successMessage.value = "事件已清空"
                }
                .onFailure { e ->
                    _errorMessage.value = "清空失败: ${e.message}"
                }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 手动刷新事件
     */
    fun refreshEvents(limit: Int = 50) {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            repository.getEvents(limit)
                .onSuccess { _events.value = it }
                .onFailure { e ->
                    _errorMessage.value = "获取事件失败: ${e.message}"
                }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 刷新状态
     */
    fun refreshStatus() {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            repository.getStatus()
                .onSuccess { _status.value = it }
                .onFailure { e ->
                    Log.w(TAG, "Refresh status failed: ${e.message}")
                }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 切换包名选中状态
     */
    fun togglePackageSelection(packageName: String) {
        val current = _selectedPackages.value.toMutableSet()
        if (current.contains(packageName)) {
            current.remove(packageName)
        } else {
            current.add(packageName)
        }
        _selectedPackages.value = current
    }

    /**
     * 加载已安装应用列表
     */
    fun loadInstalledApps(includeSystem: Boolean = false) {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            try {
                val apps = repository.getInstalledApps(includeSystem)
                _installedApps.value = apps
            } catch (e: Exception) {
                Log.e(TAG, "Load installed apps failed", e)
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 清除错误消息
     */
    fun clearError() {
        _errorMessage.value = null
    }

    /**
     * 清除成功消息
     */
    fun clearSuccess() {
        _successMessage.value = null
    }

    /**
     * 导出事件为文本格式
     */
    fun exportEventsAsText(): String {
        val events = _events.value
        val sb = StringBuilder()
        sb.appendLine("=== SVC Tracer Events Export ===")
        sb.appendLine("Total: ${events.size} events")
        sb.appendLine("Exported at: ${System.currentTimeMillis()}")
        sb.appendLine("================================")
        sb.appendLine()

        events.forEach { event ->
            sb.appendLine("#${event.id} | ${event.formatTimestamp()}")
            sb.appendLine("  PID: ${event.pid} TID: ${event.tid} UID: ${event.uid}")
            sb.appendLine("  Process: ${event.processName}")
            sb.appendLine("  Syscall: ${event.syscallName} (${event.syscallNr}) -> ${event.returnValue}")
            sb.appendLine("  Category: ${event.category}")
            if (event.args.isNotEmpty()) {
                sb.appendLine("  Args: ${event.args.joinToString(", ")}")
            }
            sb.appendLine("  Caller: ${event.callerAddr}")
            event.backtrace?.let { bt ->
                sb.appendLine("  Backtrace:")
                bt.forEach { frame -> sb.appendLine("    $frame") }
            }
            sb.appendLine()
        }

        return sb.toString()
    }

    // ==================== 内部方法 ====================

    /**
     * 加载初始数据
     */
    private fun loadInitialData() {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            // 并行加载状态和配置
            launch {
                repository.getStatus().onSuccess { _status.value = it }
            }
            launch {
                repository.getConfig().onSuccess { _config.value = it }
            }
            launch {
                repository.getStats().onSuccess { _stats.value = it }
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 开始轮询
     */
    private fun startPolling() {
        stopPolling()

        statusPollJob = viewModelScope.launch {
            repository.pollStatus()
                .catch { e -> Log.e(TAG, "Status poll error", e) }
                .collect { result ->
                    result.onSuccess { _status.value = it }
                }
        }

        eventsPollJob = viewModelScope.launch {
            repository.pollEvents()
                .catch { e -> Log.e(TAG, "Events poll error", e) }
                .collect { result ->
                    result.onSuccess { _events.value = it }
                }
        }

        statsPollJob = viewModelScope.launch {
            repository.pollStats()
                .catch { e -> Log.e(TAG, "Stats poll error", e) }
                .collect { result ->
                    result.onSuccess { _stats.value = it }
                }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 停止轮询
     */
    private fun stopPolling() {
        statusPollJob?.cancel()
        eventsPollJob?.cancel()
        statsPollJob?.cancel()
        statusPollJob = null
        eventsPollJob = null
        statsPollJob = null
    }

    override fun onCleared() {
        super.onCleared()
        stopPolling()
    }
}
```

### 6.5.7 DashboardScreen.kt — 仪表盘页面

```kotlin
package com.svctracer.manager.ui.screen

import androidx.compose.animation.animateColorAsState
import androidx.compose.foundation.layout.*
import androidx.compose.foundation.lazy.LazyColumn
import androidx.compose.foundation.lazy.items
import androidx.compose.foundation.text.KeyboardOptions
import androidx.compose.material.icons.Icons
import androidx.compose.material.icons.filled.*
import androidx.compose.material3.*
import androidx.compose.runtime.*
import androidx.compose.ui.Alignment
import androidx.compose.ui.Modifier
import androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color
import androidx.compose.ui.text.font.FontFamily
import androidx.compose.ui.text.font.FontWeight
import androidx.compose.ui.text.input.KeyboardType
import androidx.compose.ui.text.input.PasswordVisualTransformation
import androidx.compose.ui.text.input.VisualTransformation
import androidx.compose.ui.text.style.TextOverflow
import androidx.compose.ui.unit.dp
import androidx.compose.ui.unit.sp
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.SvcEvent
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.TracerStatus
import com.svctracer.manager.ui.MainViewModel

/**
 * 仪表盘页面 — 应用主页
 *
 * 显示内容：
 * - SuperKey 输入与连接控制
 * - 模块运行状态概览
 * - 统计数据卡片（事件数、缓冲区使用率等）
 * - 启动/停止控制按钮
 * - 最近事件列表预览
 */
@Composable
fun DashboardScreen(viewModel: MainViewModel) {
    val status by viewModel.status.collectAsState()
    val isConnected by viewModel.isConnected.collectAsState()
    val isLoading by viewModel.isLoading.collectAsState()
    val events by viewModel.events.collectAsState()
    val stats by viewModel.stats.collectAsState()
    val superKeyInput by viewModel.superKeyInput.collectAsState()
    val errorMessage by viewModel.errorMessage.collectAsState()
    val successMessage by viewModel.successMessage.collectAsState()

    val snackbarHostState = remember { SnackbarHostState() }

    // 显示错误/成功消息
    LaunchedEffect(errorMessage) {
        errorMessage?.let {
            snackbarHostState.showSnackbar(it, duration = SnackbarDuration.Short)
            viewModel.clearError()
        }
    }
    LaunchedEffect(successMessage) {
        successMessage?.let {
            snackbarHostState.showSnackbar(it, duration = SnackbarDuration.Short)
            viewModel.clearSuccess()
        }
    }

    Scaffold(snackbarHost = { SnackbarHost(snackbarHostState) }) { padding ->
        LazyColumn(
            modifier = Modifier
                .fillMaxSize()
                .padding(padding)
                .padding(horizontal = 16.dp),
            verticalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(12.dp),
            contentPadding = PaddingValues(vertical = 16.dp)
        ) {
            // SuperKey 输入卡片
            item {
                SuperKeyInputCard(
                    superKey = superKeyInput,
                    onSuperKeyChange = viewModel::updateSuperKeyInput,
                    onConnect = viewModel::connect,
                    onDisconnect = viewModel::disconnect,
                    isConnected = isConnected,
                    isLoading = isLoading
                )
            }

            // 连接状态指示
            if (isConnected) {
                // 状态卡片
                item {
                    ConnectionStateCard(status = status)
                }

                // 模块信息卡片
                item {
                    ModuleStatusCard(status = status)
                }

                // 统计卡片行
                item {
                    Row(
                        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(12.dp)
                    ) {
                        StatCard(
                            modifier = Modifier.weight(1f),
                            title = "总事件",
                            value = status.totalEvents.toString(),
                            icon = Icons.Default.Analytics
                        )
                        StatCard(
                            modifier = Modifier.weight(1f),
                            title = "事件/秒",
                            value = String.format("%.1f", stats.eventsPerSecond),
                            icon = Icons.Default.Speed
                        )
                    }
                }

                item {
                    Row(
                        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(12.dp)
                    ) {
                        StatCard(
                            modifier = Modifier.weight(1f),
                            title = "已丢弃",
                            value = status.droppedEvents.toString(),
                            icon = Icons.Default.Warning,
                            valueColor = if (status.droppedEvents > 0)
                                MaterialTheme.colorScheme.error else Color.Unspecified
                        )
                        StatCard(
                            modifier = Modifier.weight(1f),
                            title = "监控进程",
                            value = status.monitoredPids.toString(),
                            icon = Icons.Default.Visibility
                        )
                    }
                }

                // 缓冲区使用率
                item {
                    BufferUsageCard(status = status)
                }

                // 控制按钮
                item {
                    Row(
                        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(12.dp)
                    ) {
                        Button(
                            onClick = viewModel::startTracer,
                            modifier = Modifier.weight(1f),
                            enabled = !isLoading && !status.running,
                            colors = ButtonDefaults.buttonColors(
                                containerColor = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary
                            )
                        ) {
                            Icon(Icons.Default.PlayArrow, contentDescription = null)
                            Spacer(Modifier.width(8.dp))
                            Text("启动")
                        }

                        Button(
                            onClick = viewModel::stopTracer,
                            modifier = Modifier.weight(1f),
                            enabled = !isLoading && status.running,
                            colors = ButtonDefaults.buttonColors(
                                containerColor = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.error
                            )
                        ) {
                            Icon(Icons.Default.Stop, contentDescription = null)
                            Spacer(Modifier.width(8.dp))
                            Text("停止")
                        }
                    }
                }

                // 最近事件标题
                item {
                    Row(
                        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.SpaceBetween,
                        verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
                    ) {
                        Text(
                            "最近事件",
                            style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleMedium,
                            fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
                        )
                        TextButton(onClick = { viewModel.clearEvents() }) {
                            Text("清空")
                        }
                    }
                }

                // 最近事件列表（最多显示 10 条）
                items(events.take(10)) { event ->
                    RecentEventItem(event = event)
                }

                if (events.isEmpty()) {
                    item {
                        Card(
                            modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                            colors = CardDefaults.cardColors(
                                containerColor = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.surfaceVariant
                            )
                        ) {
                            Text(
                                "暂无事件数据",
                                modifier = Modifier
                                    .padding(24.dp)
                                    .fillMaxWidth(),
                                style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium,
                                color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
                            )
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

// ==================== 子组件 ====================

/**
 * SuperKey 输入卡片
 */
@Composable
fun SuperKeyInputCard(
    superKey: String,
    onSuperKeyChange: (String) -> Unit,
    onConnect: () -> Unit,
    onDisconnect: () -> Unit,
    isConnected: Boolean,
    isLoading: Boolean
) {
    var showPassword by remember { mutableStateOf(false) }

    Card(
        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
        elevation = CardDefaults.cardElevation(defaultElevation = 2.dp)
    ) {
        Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(16.dp)) {
            Text(
                "APatch SuperKey",
                style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleSmall,
                fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
            )
            Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))

            OutlinedTextField(
                value = superKey,
                onValueChange = onSuperKeyChange,
                modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                enabled = !isConnected,
                label = { Text("输入 SuperKey") },
                visualTransformation = if (showPassword)
                    VisualTransformation.None else PasswordVisualTransformation(),
                keyboardOptions = KeyboardOptions(keyboardType = KeyboardType.Password),
                trailingIcon = {
                    IconButton(onClick = { showPassword = !showPassword }) {
                        Icon(
                            if (showPassword) Icons.Default.VisibilityOff
                            else Icons.Default.Visibility,
                            contentDescription = "切换密码可见性"
                        )
                    }
                },
                singleLine = true
            )

            Spacer(Modifier.height(12.dp))

            if (isConnected) {
                OutlinedButton(
                    onClick = onDisconnect,
                    modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()
                ) {
                    Text("断开连接")
                }
            } else {
                Button(
                    onClick = onConnect,
                    modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                    enabled = !isLoading && superKey.isNotBlank()
                ) {
                    if (isLoading) {
                        CircularProgressIndicator(
                            modifier = Modifier.size(20.dp),
                            strokeWidth = 2.dp
                        )
                        Spacer(Modifier.width(8.dp))
                    }
                    Text("连接")
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 连接状态卡片
 */
@Composable
fun ConnectionStateCard(status: TracerStatus) {
    val statusColor by animateColorAsState(
        targetValue = if (status.running) Color(0xFF4CAF50) else Color(0xFFFF9800),
        label = "statusColor"
    )

    Card(
        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
        colors = CardDefaults.cardColors(
            containerColor = statusColor.copy(alpha = 0.1f)
        )
    ) {
        Row(
            modifier = Modifier
                .padding(16.dp)
                .fillMaxWidth(),
            verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
        ) {
            Icon(
                imageVector = if (status.running) Icons.Default.CheckCircle
                else Icons.Default.PauseCircle,
                contentDescription = null,
                tint = statusColor,
                modifier = Modifier.size(32.dp)
            )
            Spacer(Modifier.width(12.dp))
            Column {
                Text(
                    if (status.running) "追踪器运行中" else "追踪器已停止",
                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleMedium,
                    fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold,
                    color = statusColor
                )
                Text(
                    "模式: ${status.hookMode.uppercase()} | 运行时间: ${status.formatUptime()}",
                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall
                )
            }
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 模块信息卡片
 */
@Composable
fun ModuleStatusCard(status: TracerStatus) {
    Card(modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()) {
        Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(16.dp)) {
            Text(
                "模块信息",
                style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleSmall,
                fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
            )
            Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))
            InfoRow("版本", status.version)
            InfoRow("Hook 模式", status.hookMode.uppercase())
            InfoRow("文件日志", if (status.fileLogging) "启用" else "禁用")
            if (status.fileLogging && status.logPath.isNotEmpty()) {
                InfoRow("日志路径", status.logPath)
            }
        }
    }
}

@Composable
fun InfoRow(label: String, value: String) {
    Row(
        modifier = Modifier
            .fillMaxWidth()
            .padding(vertical = 2.dp),
        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.SpaceBetween
    ) {
        Text(label, style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium, color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant)
        Text(value, style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium, fontWeight = FontWeight.Medium)
    }
}

/**
 * 统计数据卡片
 */
@Composable
fun StatCard(
    modifier: Modifier = Modifier,
    title: String,
    value: String,
    icon: ImageVector,
    valueColor: Color = Color.Unspecified
) {
    Card(modifier = modifier) {
        Column(
            modifier = Modifier.padding(16.dp),
            horizontalAlignment = Alignment.CenterHorizontally
        ) {
            Icon(
                icon,
                contentDescription = null,
                tint = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary,
                modifier = Modifier.size(24.dp)
            )
            Spacer(Modifier.height(4.dp))
            Text(
                value,
                style = MaterialTheme.typography.headlineSmall,
                fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold,
                color = if (valueColor != Color.Unspecified) valueColor
                else MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurface
            )
            Text(
                title,
                style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall,
                color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
            )
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 缓冲区使用率卡片
 */
@Composable
fun BufferUsageCard(status: TracerStatus) {
    Card(modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()) {
        Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(16.dp)) {
            Row(
                modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.SpaceBetween
            ) {
                Text("缓冲区使用率", style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleSmall)
                Text(
                    "${status.bufferEvents}/${status.bufferCapacity}",
                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall
                )
            }
            Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))
            LinearProgressIndicator(
                progress = { status.bufferUsagePercent / 100f },
                modifier = Modifier
                    .fillMaxWidth()
                    .height(8.dp),
                color = when {
                    status.bufferUsagePercent > 90f -> MaterialTheme.colorScheme.error
                    status.bufferUsagePercent > 70f -> Color(0xFFFF9800)
                    else -> MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary
                }
            )
            Spacer(Modifier.height(4.dp))
            Text(
                String.format("%.1f%%", status.bufferUsagePercent),
                style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall,
                color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
            )
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 最近事件列表项
 */
@Composable
fun RecentEventItem(event: SvcEvent) {
    Card(
        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
        colors = CardDefaults.cardColors(
            containerColor = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.surfaceVariant
        )
    ) {
        Row(
            modifier = Modifier
                .padding(12.dp)
                .fillMaxWidth(),
            verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
        ) {
            // 分类颜色指示器
            Surface(
                modifier = Modifier.size(8.dp),
                shape = MaterialTheme.shapes.extraSmall,
                color = when (event.category) {
                    "file_io" -> Color(0xFF2196F3)
                    "network" -> Color(0xFF4CAF50)
                    "process" -> Color(0xFFFF9800)
                    "ipc" -> Color(0xFF9C27B0)
                    "memory" -> Color(0xFFE91E63)
                    "signal" -> Color(0xFF00BCD4)
                    else -> Color.Gray
                }
            ) {}

            Spacer(Modifier.width(8.dp))

            Column(modifier = Modifier.weight(1f)) {
                Text(
                    "${event.processName} (PID: ${event.pid})",
                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium,
                    fontWeight = FontWeight.Medium,
                    maxLines = 1,
                    overflow = TextOverflow.Ellipsis
                )
                Text(
                    "${event.syscallName} -> ${event.returnValue}",
                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall,
                    fontFamily = FontFamily.Monospace,
                    fontSize = 12.sp
                )
            }

            Column(horizontalAlignment = Alignment.End) {
                Text(
                    event.categoryDisplayName(),
                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.labelSmall,
                    color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary
                )
                Text(
                    event.formatTimestamp().takeLast(12),
                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.labelSmall,
                    fontFamily = FontFamily.Monospace,
                    color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
                )
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.5.8 ConfigScreen.kt — 配置管理页面

```kotlin
package com.svctracer.manager.ui.screen

import androidx.compose.foundation.layout.*
import androidx.compose.foundation.lazy.LazyColumn
import androidx.compose.foundation.lazy.items
import androidx.compose.foundation.selection.selectable
import androidx.compose.foundation.selection.selectableGroup
import androidx.compose.foundation.text.KeyboardOptions
import androidx.compose.material.icons.Icons
import androidx.compose.material.icons.filled.Search
import androidx.compose.material3.*
import androidx.compose.runtime.*
import androidx.compose.ui.Alignment
import androidx.compose.ui.Modifier
import androidx.compose.ui.semantics.Role
import androidx.compose.ui.text.font.FontWeight
import androidx.compose.ui.text.input.KeyboardType
import androidx.compose.ui.unit.dp
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.TracerConfig
import com.svctracer.manager.ui.MainViewModel

/**
 * 配置管理页面
 *
 * 提供完整的追踪配置界面，包括：
 * - 目标应用选择（带搜索过滤）
 * - PID/UID 手动输入
 * - Hook 模式选择（Slim/All/Range）
 * - 事件分类过滤
 * - 日志记录选项
 * - 反调试绕过开关
 */
@Composable
fun ConfigScreen(viewModel: MainViewModel) {
    val config by viewModel.config.collectAsState()
    val isConnected by viewModel.isConnected.collectAsState()
    val isLoading by viewModel.isLoading.collectAsState()
    val installedApps by viewModel.installedApps.collectAsState()
    val selectedPackages by viewModel.selectedPackages.collectAsState()

    // 本地配置状态（用户编辑中的值，点击"应用"后同步到 ViewModel）
    var hookMode by remember(config) { mutableStateOf(config.hookMode) }
    var rangeStart by remember(config) { mutableStateOf(config.syscallRangeStart.toString()) }
    var rangeEnd by remember(config) { mutableStateOf(config.syscallRangeEnd.toString()) }
    var logArgs by remember(config) { mutableStateOf(config.logArgs) }
    var logReturn by remember(config) { mutableStateOf(config.logReturn) }
    var logBacktrace by remember(config) { mutableStateOf(config.logBacktrace) }
    var fileLogging by remember(config) { mutableStateOf(config.fileLogging) }
    var logFilePath by remember(config) { mutableStateOf(config.logFilePath) }
    var antiDebugBypass by remember(config) { mutableStateOf(config.antiDebugBypass) }
    var pidInput by remember { mutableStateOf(config.targetPids.joinToString(", ")) }
    var uidInput by remember { mutableStateOf(config.targetUids.joinToString(", ")) }
    var appSearchQuery by remember { mutableStateOf("") }

    // 事件分类状态
    val allCategories = listOf("file_io", "network", "process", "ipc", "memory", "signal")
    val categoryNames = mapOf(
        "file_io" to "File I/O",
        "network" to "Network",
        "process" to "Process",
        "ipc" to "IPC",
        "memory" to "Memory",
        "signal" to "Signal"
    )
    var enabledCategories by remember(config) {
        mutableStateOf(config.categories.toSet())
    }

    // 加载应用列表
    LaunchedEffect(isConnected) {
        if (isConnected) {
            viewModel.loadInstalledApps()
        }
    }

    LazyColumn(
        modifier = Modifier
            .fillMaxSize()
            .padding(horizontal = 16.dp),
        verticalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(12.dp),
        contentPadding = PaddingValues(vertical = 16.dp)
    ) {
        // 连接状态检查
        if (!isConnected) {
            item {
                Card(
                    modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                    colors = CardDefaults.cardColors(
                        containerColor = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.errorContainer
                    )
                ) {
                    Text(
                        "请先在仪表盘页面连接到 KPM 模块",
                        modifier = Modifier.padding(16.dp),
                        color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onErrorContainer
                    )
                }
            }
            return@LazyColumn
        }

        // === 目标应用选择 ===
        item {
            Card(modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()) {
                Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(16.dp)) {
                    Text(
                        "目标应用",
                        style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleSmall,
                        fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
                    )
                    Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))

                    OutlinedTextField(
                        value = appSearchQuery,
                        onValueChange = { appSearchQuery = it },
                        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                        placeholder = { Text("搜索应用...") },
                        leadingIcon = { Icon(Icons.Default.Search, null) },
                        singleLine = true
                    )

                    Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))

                    // 过滤后的应用列表（最多显示 20 个）
                    val filteredApps = installedApps.filter { (pkg, _, name) ->
                        appSearchQuery.isBlank() ||
                                pkg.contains(appSearchQuery, ignoreCase = true) ||
                                name.contains(appSearchQuery, ignoreCase = true)
                    }.take(20)

                    filteredApps.forEach { (pkg, uid, name) ->
                        Row(
                            modifier = Modifier
                                .fillMaxWidth()
                                .padding(vertical = 4.dp),
                            verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
                        ) {
                            Checkbox(
                                checked = selectedPackages.contains(pkg),
                                onCheckedChange = { viewModel.togglePackageSelection(pkg) }
                            )
                            Column(modifier = Modifier.weight(1f)) {
                                Text(name, style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium)
                                Text(
                                    "$pkg (UID: $uid)",
                                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall,
                                    color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
                                )
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    if (selectedPackages.isNotEmpty()) {
                        Spacer(Modifier.height(4.dp))
                        Text(
                            "已选择 ${selectedPackages.size} 个应用",
                            style = MaterialTheme.typography.labelSmall,
                            color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary
                        )
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        // === PID/UID 手动输入 ===
        item {
            Card(modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()) {
                Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(16.dp)) {
                    Text(
                        "手动过滤",
                        style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleSmall,
                        fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
                    )
                    Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))

                    OutlinedTextField(
                        value = pidInput,
                        onValueChange = { pidInput = it },
                        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                        label = { Text("目标 PID（逗号分隔）") },
                        placeholder = { Text("例如: 1234, 5678") },
                        keyboardOptions = KeyboardOptions(keyboardType = KeyboardType.Number),
                        singleLine = true
                    )
                    Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))

                    OutlinedTextField(
                        value = uidInput,
                        onValueChange = { uidInput = it },
                        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                        label = { Text("目标 UID（逗号分隔）") },
                        placeholder = { Text("例如: 10123, 10456") },
                        keyboardOptions = KeyboardOptions(keyboardType = KeyboardType.Number),
                        singleLine = true
                    )
                }
            }
        }

        // === Hook 模式 ===
        item {
            Card(modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()) {
                Column(
                    modifier = Modifier
                        .padding(16.dp)
                        .selectableGroup()
                ) {
                    Text(
                        "Hook 模式",
                        style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleSmall,
                        fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
                    )
                    Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))

                    listOf(
                        "slim" to "Slim — 仅监控关键 SVC 调用（推荐）",
                        "all" to "All — 监控所有 SVC 调用（高开销）",
                        "range" to "Range — 监控指定范围的 SVC 号"
                    ).forEach { (mode, label) ->
                        Row(
                            modifier = Modifier
                                .fillMaxWidth()
                                .selectable(
                                    selected = hookMode == mode,
                                    onClick = { hookMode = mode },
                                    role = Role.RadioButton
                                )
                                .padding(vertical = 4.dp),
                            verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
                        ) {
                            RadioButton(
                                selected = hookMode == mode,
                                onClick = null
                            )
                            Spacer(Modifier.width(8.dp))
                            Text(label, style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium)
                        }
                    }

                    // Range 模式的范围输入
                    if (hookMode == "range") {
                        Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))
                        Row(
                            modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                            horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(8.dp)
                        ) {
                            OutlinedTextField(
                                value = rangeStart,
                                onValueChange = { rangeStart = it },
                                modifier = Modifier.weight(1f),
                                label = { Text("起始 SVC 号") },
                                keyboardOptions = KeyboardOptions(keyboardType = KeyboardType.Number),
                                singleLine = true
                            )
                            OutlinedTextField(
                                value = rangeEnd,
                                onValueChange = { rangeEnd = it },
                                modifier = Modifier.weight(1f),
                                label = { Text("结束 SVC 号") },
                                keyboardOptions = KeyboardOptions(keyboardType = KeyboardType.Number),
                                singleLine = true
                            )
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        // === 事件分类 ===
        item {
            Card(modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()) {
                Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(16.dp)) {
                    Text(
                        "事件分类过滤",
                        style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleSmall,
                        fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
                    )
                    Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))

                    // 使用 FlowRow 效果的网格布局
                    allCategories.chunked(3).forEach { row ->
                        Row(
                            modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                            horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(4.dp)
                        ) {
                            row.forEach { category ->
                                Row(
                                    modifier = Modifier.weight(1f),
                                    verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
                                ) {
                                    Checkbox(
                                        checked = enabledCategories.contains(category),
                                        onCheckedChange = { checked ->
                                            enabledCategories = if (checked) {
                                                enabledCategories + category
                                            } else {
                                                enabledCategories - category
                                            }
                                        }
                                    )
                                    Text(
                                        categoryNames[category] ?: category,
                                        style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall
                                    )
                                }
                            }
                            // 填充空白（如果行不满 3 个）
                            repeat(3 - row.size) {
                                Spacer(modifier = Modifier.weight(1f))
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        // === 日志选项 ===
        item {
            Card(modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()) {
                Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(16.dp)) {
                    Text(
                        "日志记录选项",
                        style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleSmall,
                        fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
                    )
                    Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))

                    SwitchRow("记录调用参数", logArgs) { logArgs = it }
                    SwitchRow("记录返回值", logReturn) { logReturn = it }
                    SwitchRow("记录调用栈（高开销）", logBacktrace) { logBacktrace = it }
                    HorizontalDivider(modifier = Modifier.padding(vertical = 4.dp))
                    SwitchRow("启用文件日志", fileLogging) { fileLogging = it }

                    if (fileLogging) {
                        Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))
                        OutlinedTextField(
                            value = logFilePath,
                            onValueChange = { logFilePath = it },
                            modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                            label = { Text("日志文件路径") },
                            singleLine = true
                        )
                    }

                    HorizontalDivider(modifier = Modifier.padding(vertical = 4.dp))
                    SwitchRow("反调试绕过", antiDebugBypass) { antiDebugBypass = it }
                }
            }
        }

        // === 应用配置按钮 ===
        item {
            Button(
                onClick = {
                    val newConfig = TracerConfig(
                        targetPids = pidInput.split(",")
                            .mapNotNull { it.trim().toIntOrNull() },
                        targetUids = uidInput.split(",")
                            .mapNotNull { it.trim().toIntOrNull() },
                        targetPackages = selectedPackages.toList(),
                        hookMode = hookMode,
                        syscallRangeStart = rangeStart.toIntOrNull() ?: 0,
                        syscallRangeEnd = rangeEnd.toIntOrNull() ?: 500,
                        categories = enabledCategories.toList(),
                        logArgs = logArgs,
                        logReturn = logReturn,
                        logBacktrace = logBacktrace,
                        fileLogging = fileLogging,
                        logFilePath = logFilePath,
                        antiDebugBypass = antiDebugBypass,
                        bufferSize = config.bufferSize
                    )
                    viewModel.applyConfig(newConfig)
                },
                modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                enabled = !isLoading
            ) {
                if (isLoading) {
                    CircularProgressIndicator(
                        modifier = Modifier.size(20.dp),
                        strokeWidth = 2.dp,
                        color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onPrimary
                    )
                    Spacer(Modifier.width(8.dp))
                }
                Text("应用配置")
            }
        }

        // 底部间距
        item { Spacer(Modifier.height(16.dp)) }
    }
}

/**
 * 开关行组件
 */
@Composable
fun SwitchRow(label: String, checked: Boolean, onCheckedChange: (Boolean) -> Unit) {
    Row(
        modifier = Modifier
            .fillMaxWidth()
            .padding(vertical = 4.dp),
        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.SpaceBetween,
        verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
    ) {
        Text(label, style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium)
        Switch(checked = checked, onCheckedChange = onCheckedChange)
    }
}
```

### 6.5.9 LogViewerScreen.kt — 日志查看器页面

```kotlin
package com.svctracer.manager.ui.screen

import android.content.Context
import android.content.Intent
import android.net.Uri
import androidx.compose.animation.AnimatedVisibility
import androidx.compose.foundation.clickable
import androidx.compose.foundation.horizontalScroll
import androidx.compose.foundation.layout.*
import androidx.compose.foundation.lazy.LazyColumn
import androidx.compose.foundation.lazy.items
import androidx.compose.foundation.lazy.rememberLazyListState
import androidx.compose.foundation.rememberScrollState
import androidx.compose.material.icons.Icons
import androidx.compose.material.icons.filled.*
import androidx.compose.material3.*
import androidx.compose.runtime.*
import androidx.compose.ui.Alignment
import androidx.compose.ui.Modifier
import androidx.compose.ui.platform.LocalContext
import androidx.compose.ui.text.font.FontFamily
import androidx.compose.ui.text.font.FontWeight
import androidx.compose.ui.text.style.TextOverflow
import androidx.compose.ui.unit.dp
import androidx.compose.ui.unit.sp
import androidx.core.content.FileProvider
import com.svctracer.manager.data.model.SvcEvent
import com.svctracer.manager.ui.MainViewModel
import java.io.File

/**
 * 日志查看器页面
 *
 * 提供完整的事件日志浏览与分析功能：
 * - 实时事件列表（可展开查看详情）
 * - 搜索过滤（按进程名、SVC 名称）
 * - 分类过滤（File I/O、Network、Process 等）
 * - 自动刷新控制
 * - 导出功能（通过 FileProvider 分享）
 */
@OptIn(ExperimentalMaterial3Api::class)
@Composable
fun LogViewerScreen(viewModel: MainViewModel) {
    val events by viewModel.events.collectAsState()
    val isConnected by viewModel.isConnected.collectAsState()

    var searchQuery by remember { mutableStateOf("") }
    var selectedCategory by remember { mutableStateOf("all") }
    var autoRefresh by remember { mutableStateOf(true) }
    var refreshInterval by remember { mutableStateOf(2f) }

    val context = LocalContext.current
    val listState = rememberLazyListState()

    val categories = listOf(
        "all" to "全部",
        "file_io" to "File I/O",
        "network" to "Network",
        "process" to "Process",
        "ipc" to "IPC",
        "memory" to "Memory",
        "signal" to "Signal"
    )

    // 过滤事件
    val filteredEvents = events.filter { event ->
        val matchesSearch = searchQuery.isBlank() ||
                event.processName.contains(searchQuery, ignoreCase = true) ||
                event.syscallName.contains(searchQuery, ignoreCase = true) ||
                event.pid.toString().contains(searchQuery)
        val matchesCategory = selectedCategory == "all" || event.category == selectedCategory
        matchesSearch && matchesCategory
    }

    // 自动刷新
    LaunchedEffect(autoRefresh, refreshInterval) {
        if (autoRefresh && isConnected) {
            while (true) {
                viewModel.refreshEvents()
                kotlinx.coroutines.delay((refreshInterval * 1000).toLong())
            }
        }
    }

    Column(modifier = Modifier.fillMaxSize()) {
        // 搜索栏
        OutlinedTextField(
            value = searchQuery,
            onValueChange = { searchQuery = it },
            modifier = Modifier
                .fillMaxWidth()
                .padding(horizontal = 16.dp, vertical = 8.dp),
            placeholder = { Text("搜索事件（进程名、SVC 名称、PID）") },
            leadingIcon = { Icon(Icons.Default.Search, null) },
            trailingIcon = {
                if (searchQuery.isNotEmpty()) {
                    IconButton(onClick = { searchQuery = "" }) {
                        Icon(Icons.Default.Clear, "清除")
                    }
                }
            },
            singleLine = true
        )

        // 控制栏：自动刷新 + 导出
        Row(
            modifier = Modifier
                .fillMaxWidth()
                .padding(horizontal = 16.dp),
            horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.SpaceBetween,
            verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
        ) {
            Row(verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically) {
                Text("自动刷新", style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall)
                Switch(
                    checked = autoRefresh,
                    onCheckedChange = { autoRefresh = it },
                    modifier = Modifier.padding(horizontal = 4.dp)
                )
                if (autoRefresh) {
                    Text(
                        "${refreshInterval.toInt()}s",
                        style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall,
                        color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary
                    )
                }
            }

            Row {
                IconButton(onClick = { viewModel.refreshEvents() }) {
                    Icon(Icons.Default.Refresh, "手动刷新")
                }
                IconButton(onClick = { exportEvents(context, viewModel) }) {
                    Icon(Icons.Default.Share, "导出")
                }
            }
        }

        // 分类过滤 Chips
        Row(
            modifier = Modifier
                .fillMaxWidth()
                .horizontalScroll(rememberScrollState())
                .padding(horizontal = 16.dp, vertical = 4.dp),
            horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(8.dp)
        ) {
            categories.forEach { (key, label) ->
                FilterChip(
                    selected = selectedCategory == key,
                    onClick = { selectedCategory = key },
                    label = {
                        Text(
                            if (key == "all") "$label (${events.size})"
                            else "$label (${events.count { it.category == key }})"
                        )
                    }
                )
            }
        }

        HorizontalDivider()

        // 事件列表
        if (!isConnected) {
            Box(
                modifier = Modifier.fillMaxSize(),
                contentAlignment = Alignment.Center
            ) {
                Text(
                    "请先在仪表盘页面连接到 KPM 模块",
                    color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
                )
            }
        } else if (filteredEvents.isEmpty()) {
            Box(
                modifier = Modifier.fillMaxSize(),
                contentAlignment = Alignment.Center
            ) {
                Column(horizontalAlignment = Alignment.CenterHorizontally) {
                    Icon(
                        Icons.Default.EventNote,
                        contentDescription = null,
                        modifier = Modifier.size(48.dp),
                        tint = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
                    )
                    Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))
                    Text(
                        "暂无事件数据",
                        color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
                    )
                }
            }
        } else {
            LazyColumn(
                state = listState,
                modifier = Modifier.fillMaxSize(),
                contentPadding = PaddingValues(horizontal = 16.dp, vertical = 8.dp),
                verticalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(4.dp)
            ) {
                items(filteredEvents, key = { it.id }) { event ->
                    EventListItem(event = event)
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 可展开的事件列表项
 */
@Composable
fun EventListItem(event: SvcEvent) {
    var expanded by remember { mutableStateOf(false) }

    Card(
        modifier = Modifier
            .fillMaxWidth()
            .clickable { expanded = !expanded },
        colors = CardDefaults.cardColors(
            containerColor = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.surface
        ),
        elevation = CardDefaults.cardElevation(defaultElevation = 1.dp)
    ) {
        Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(12.dp)) {
            // 头部信息
            Row(
                modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),
                horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.SpaceBetween,
                verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
            ) {
                Text(
                    "#${event.id}",
                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.labelSmall,
                    color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary,
                    fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
                )
                Text(
                    event.formatTimestamp(),
                    style = MaterialTheme.typography.labelSmall,
                    fontFamily = FontFamily.Monospace,
                    color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
                )
            }

            Spacer(Modifier.height(4.dp))

            // 进程信息
            Text(
                "${event.processName} (PID: ${event.pid}, TID: ${event.tid})",
                style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium,
                fontWeight = FontWeight.Medium,
                maxLines = 1,
                overflow = TextOverflow.Ellipsis
            )

            // SVC 调用信息
            Text(
                "${event.syscallName} (${event.syscallNr}) -> ${event.returnValue}  [${event.categoryDisplayName()}]",
                style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall,
                fontFamily = FontFamily.Monospace,
                fontSize = 12.sp
            )

            // 展开详情
            AnimatedVisibility(visible = expanded) {
                Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(top = 8.dp)) {
                    HorizontalDivider()
                    Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))

                    Text("UID: ${event.uid}", style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall)
                    Text("Caller: ${event.callerAddr}", style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall,
                        fontFamily = FontFamily.Monospace)

                    if (event.args.isNotEmpty()) {
                        Spacer(Modifier.height(4.dp))
                        Text(
                            "参数:",
                            style = MaterialTheme.typography.labelSmall,
                            fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
                        )
                        event.args.forEachIndexed { index, arg ->
                            Text(
                                "  x$index: $arg",
                                style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall,
                                fontFamily = FontFamily.Monospace,
                                fontSize = 11.sp
                            )
                        }
                    }

                    event.backtrace?.let { bt ->
                        Spacer(Modifier.height(4.dp))
                        Text(
                            "调用栈:",
                            style = MaterialTheme.typography.labelSmall,
                            fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold
                        )
                        bt.forEach { frame ->
                            Text(
                                "  $frame",
                                style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodySmall,
                                fontFamily = FontFamily.Monospace,
                                fontSize = 11.sp
                            )
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            // 展开/收起指示
            Icon(
                if (expanded) Icons.Default.ExpandLess else Icons.Default.ExpandMore,
                contentDescription = null,
                modifier = Modifier
                    .fillMaxWidth()
                    .size(16.dp),
                tint = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant
            )
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 导出事件到文件并分享
 */
private fun exportEvents(context: Context, viewModel: MainViewModel) {
    val text = viewModel.exportEventsAsText()
    val file = File(context.cacheDir, "svc_events_export.txt")
    file.writeText(text)

    val uri: Uri = FileProvider.getUriForFile(
        context,
        "${context.packageName}.fileprovider",
        file
    )

    val intent = Intent(Intent.ACTION_SEND).apply {
        type = "text/plain"
        putExtra(Intent.EXTRA_STREAM, uri)
        addFlags(Intent.FLAG_GRANT_READ_URI_PERMISSION)
    }
    context.startActivity(Intent.createChooser(intent, "导出 SVC 事件日志"))
}
```
